            <div class="_8t03 _8tm_">
             <a class="_8ulx" href="/groups/795724047209616/">
              <div class="_8uly">
               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 北美華人哩程交流討論
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 本社團起源於對航空公司哩程計畫/信用卡點數轉換航空公司哩程計畫的喜好，有鑒於哩程計畫/信用卡點數資訊的複雜與混亂，想要提供一個地方讓大家可以互相討論，分享關於如何累積並且善用航空公司的哩程及信用卡點數，同時提供一個讓大家可以分享旅遊相關的經驗的園地。 服務對象為：對哩程計畫／信用卡點數感興趣的華人及其配偶 ✴️快速連結 ✴️ 1. 新手發問前請先社團懶人包： https://www.facebook.com/groups/milestaiwan/permalink/816089865173034/ 或是TripPlus部落格終極懶人包 http://blog.tripplus.cc/2404/allinone-tutorial 2. Blog鏈結，教學文章都在這邊： http://blog.tripplus.cc/ 3. 粉絲團鏈結，特價機票會公告在這： https://www.facebook.com/tripplus.cc/ 4. 信用卡referral link專區（七月）： https://www.facebook.com/groups/milestaiwan/permalink/2279195628862443/ 5. Amex信用卡航空退額DP帖（不停更新）： https://www.facebook.com/groups/milestaiwan/permalink/1550543531727660/ 6. 續卡禮資料大集合 (Retention Offer)（不停更新）： https://www.facebook.com/groups/milestaiwan/permalink/1550607195054627/ 7. 發問專區（求救及尋求建議專區）七月：https://www.facebook.com/groups/milestaiwan/permalink/2279190615529611/ 8. 信用卡點數轉點航空計畫所需時間DP帖：https://www.facebook.com/groups/milestaiwan/permalink/1907482819367061/ ❗️重要公告 ❗️ 1. 本社團即日起禁止所有交易文，及MS（假消費）相關討論文。 2. 本社團即日起針對客服文及很明顯可以在置頂文找到答案的Post，不告知一律刪文。 3. 本社團即日起對於明顯的客服文、伸手文、沒有實際範例、前因後果描述不清或是內容沒有超過四行（電腦版）或 八行（手機版）的「發問文」，會關閉回應及刪除，接著請發問者移駕到 #發問專區 詢問，前後因果描述清楚及帶有範例的發問文，允許直接Po在版上發問。 4. 本社團重視言論自由，重視每個人的分享，請尊重他人提供之DP，連續酸人、發布人身攻擊言論、喜歡吵架且不聽勸導者，版主得基於社團良好風氣，不告知馬上刪除團員資格。 5. 為鼓勵團友分享資訊，所有的分享/討論文（「發問文」依然需遵守四行文版規規定），只要發文的主體內帶有任何跟「信用卡申請及使用」「點數系統累積及使用」「旅遊過程行程資訊及延伸的景點/餐廳介紹」「航空哩程獲得及使用」「飯店住宿體驗心得」「飛行體驗心得」「貴賓室體驗心得」相關的資訊，皆從寬認定，都允許發在版上，不關文也不刪文。 6. 本社團每半年會進行一次成員大掃除，對於毫無互動的團友（互動的定義包含：發文分享自己的旅遊經驗、里程及點數的經驗、分享資訊/DP、看到分享好資訊的團友回文鼓勵一下，按個讚，都算在互動的範圍之內），我們會將成員自社團名單中移除。 7. 連續在社團內引戰或是與別人吵架者，不告知馬上刪除團員資格。 ⛔️社團要求更改及刪除 貼文/留言 規則 ⛔️ 1. 未經與允許的廣告文、交易文及任何形式的政治文：不告知馬上刪除。 2. MS相關文：不告知馬上刪除。 3. 「發問」文行數限制（電腦版四行滿版 或 手機版八行滿版，大家好、謝謝、空白及換行不列入行數計算）：柔性勸導轉發發問專區後刪除。 4. 個人抱怨文，請發自己的牆上：不告知馬上刪除。 5. 酸文、引戰文、人身攻擊文：不告知馬上刪除 6. 爭議性言論：管理群的責任在於維持社團內的秩序，由於爭議詞彙每個人的認知不一樣，管理群不應該也無法對所有的爭議詞彙列管，管理群僅會就「負面且在社團內發生過多次爭吵的詞彙」列管並給予柔性勸導，其餘版友自行認知為爭議詞彙的部分，應先行予發文/留言者溝通，這是屬於大家的園地，只有溝通才有助於雙方互相了解進而避免紛爭，管理群「僅會在爭吵發生時」才介入處理。團友在溝通過程中，請理性討論，任何人身攻擊、主動引戰、謾罵、酸言酸語言論，攻擊者會被警告，發生兩次以上者，（發文者若多次發相同詞彙，引發多次爭吵，也依相同方法處置），依據板規刪除團員資格。 7. 分享新聞／外部連結：不帶有兩行以上的個人評論的貼文，將會一律刪除。 8. 純照片分享文：不管照片是不是有跟社團主題相關的資訊，只要引文無內容，或是只有過於簡單且明顯無意義的資訊（像是：這太漂亮了、驚呆了、百聞不如一見 ... etc），一律關文宣導，要求在引言內補充相關資訊，相關補充資訊只要帶有：「信用卡申請及使用」「點數系統累積及使用」「旅遊過程行程資訊及延伸的景點/餐廳介紹」「航空哩程獲得及使用」「飯店住宿體驗心得」「飛行體驗心得」「貴賓室體驗心得」資訊即可。 ⚠️其他重要版規，若無法認同請勿加入 ⚠️ 1. 為維護社團正常運作以及保障大多數團員權益, 本社團保留刪除留言與取消團員資格之權力，若有在團外散播詆毀社團的言論，不告知直接刪除團員資格。 2. 本社團謝絕政治相關貼文, 屢勸不聽者將刪除團員資格。 3. 本社團謝絕違犯善良風俗的貼文, 屢勸不聽者將刪除團員資格。 4. 本社團謝絕個人抱怨的貼文, 請張貼在自己的Timeline，負面經驗分享文由於太容易引起爭吵，社團管理員保留刪除的權利，並會視情況刪除。 5. 本社團禁止攬客行為，不限型式，違者一律刪文刪人! 6. 本社團禁止同屬性社團的廣告，不限型式，違者一律刪文，累犯刪人! 7. 請勿張貼賺點擊率之相關連結網頁，違者一律刪文，累犯刪人! 8. 請勿封鎖管理員, 一經發現立即刪除團員資格, 不另通知(也無法通知)。 9. 請勿拒絕讓管理員回文，一經發現立即刪除團員資格。 10. 此為非公開性社團，所有團友的發言與討論，為保護著作權，未經作者、所有推文者及版主同意，不得轉錄。經作者、推文者及版主同意得轉錄者，需以保存事實全貌為原則，完整轉錄文章。違反者將於告知後刪除成員資格。 11. 本社團不禁止推廣個人粉絲專頁及Blog，但是須經審核，分享主題需與社團主題相關且符合管理員訂立之推廣文發文格式（請聯絡管理員獲得此資訊）所有未經審核的粉專及Blog推廣文，不另行通知，一概刪除，管理員保留最終核准及刪文權利，經核准之宣傳文，社團不替其粉專／Blog的行為背書。 12. 請勿用多重帳號加入社團，經查實後，不告知刪除並封鎖所有帳號團員資格。
                </div>

                 歐洲旅遊・我在歐洲自由行🇬🇧英🇫🇷法🇪🇸西🇮🇹義🇩🇪德🇨🇭瑞.歐洲各國
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 入社團請 #不要 貼感謝文，直接到此自我介紹一下吧！跟大家講你來自哪裡，去過哪些歐洲國家，最喜歡哪？ ⬇必讀版規⬇ 歡迎加入『我在』系列社團，請閱讀以下社團規則： SHARE - 歡迎大家群內直接分享有歐洲有關旅遊訊息(不建議轉貼粉專)，版上“禁止”任何商業貼文及(類似)商業、旅遊帳號來分享，社團內部直接分享圖片及文字和文章優先發布，請不要私訊版主為何貼文還未發佈，最重要的是遵照版規貼文。 SEARCH - 大家請多多互相討論與社團相關問題，並且善用搜尋功能看之前有沒有發問過，避免重複問過的問題。 POLITE - 有些人或許問題你覺得很基本，可以提醒去搜尋版內文章或Google，或者你願意幫忙就幫，但不要口出惡言。 本社團嚴禁內容農場文章及直銷入團宣傳，所有人貼文前請詳讀易下細則： （1）有任何問題都直接在版上討論，“勿”直接私訊對方，並“嚴禁”在版上留下或索取電話及line與任何通訊方式，已有版友險遭詐騙，請謹慎。 （2）一人每七天”限制”張貼一次貼文，相同主題請盡量在同一篇分享，不要分好幾篇張貼，避免過於頻繁貼文。未審核過貼文還繼續轉發其他貼文，全部直接刪除。 （3）本社團所有貼文及轉貼文敘述若空白/過短(少於五行)/直接複製原文，直接刪除。 （4）請"不要"放自拍或一大堆個人照，只歡迎旅遊當地風俗民情景點照！貼文未展開前顯示超過一張個人照片刪除，如果只有一張圖，就不能是臉照，抱歉，太多人把這當寫真集在張貼。 （5）此社團不適合張貼任何宣傳，貼文(包含原文中)內若有商業/旅遊粉絲頁/旅遊line群/旅遊社團/民宿/活動，貼文都直接刪除。 （6）單純只想吸引粉絲的貼文，標籤粉專，叫大家按讚、私訊、加好友、分享的貼文會被刪除。 （7）提及香菸貼文請附上所有健康警語：「吸菸有害健康」、「吸菸會導致癌症」、「吸菸能導致肺癌、心臟血管疾病及肺氣腫」、「孕婦吸菸易導致胎兒早產及體重不足」、「吸菸害人害己」、「戒菸可減少健康的危害」，提及酒類貼文請附上以下兩條警語：「禁止酒駕」、「飲酒過量，有害健康」。但禁止有任何菸酒推廣貼文。 （8）討論性貼文(非轉貼)優先審核，其他貼文統一每週審核一次，貼文或原文內若內含導購連結則刪除封鎖。 （9）使用自己或他人帳號設法把自己貼文往上推，增加曝光，會將所有涉入帳號封鎖。 （10）新社友一個月內不能張貼新文，貼文者會被刪除退群，但可以回覆別人貼文互動。請先觀摩別人怎麼貼文。 （11）由於許多不佳的案例，本系列社團一律禁止徵旅伴。 歡迎全球中文人士入社團，此外，使用粵語中文時大家會比較看不懂，建議貼文下面再來個白話中文版本。 所有貼文開頭請按照規定發文，在ㄧ開頭(主標題)加上主題標籤 #我在XX自由行 如果你的貼文不單一講歐洲哪個國家，XX就填上歐洲，如果你在德國自由行，XX就填上德國，你想特別講哪個城市，XX可以填上柏林，範例如下： #我在歐洲自由行 #我在德國自由行 #我在柏林自由行 想加入以下line群組朋友，請加此官方帳號，留下您的line帳號及想加入line群和加入理由(缺一不可)，記得要開放line帳號搜尋，管理員會於一週內加您入群。 🌍我在歐洲自由行 🌎我在美洲自由行 🌏我在亞洲自由行 🌍我在非洲中東土耳其自由行 🌏我在大洋洲自由行 🦉我在Wozai官方line帳號（搜尋@wozai.travel）🦉 https://lin.ee/ubfJia7 🦉我在歐洲自由行telegram群🦉 https://t.me/joinchat/RJZZ9RiHSRXhuseldUnegA 臉書社團 🍇我在歐洲自由行 https://www.facebook.com/groups/travler.europe/ 🍇我在亞洲自由行 https://www.facebook.com/groups/wozai.asia/ 🍇我在美洲自由行 https://www.facebook.com/groups/wozai.america/ 🍇我在大洋洲自由行 https://www.facebook.com/groups/wozai.oceania/ 🍇 我在非洲.中東.土耳其自由行 https://www.facebook.com/groups/wozai.mea/ 🍇 我在英法自由行 https://www.facebook.com/groups/wozai/ 🌈 國外旅遊景點票券購買 Klook https://goo.gl/YBTfzJ 🌈 倫敦音樂劇線上購票 https://ukfrtravel.londontheatredirect.com 歡迎到官網 https://wozai-travel.com/ 討論分享！ Instagram: www.instagram.com/wozai.travel 有很多漂亮風景照片喔！

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 社團簡介 歡迎大家加入這個全新風格的台灣人社團，不管你是來異鄉幾天，幾個月，或是好多年，這個社團成立的目的就是要讓海外打拚生活的台灣遊子們有一個屬於我們自己的園地，可以在此放心，安心，開心去串聯我們彼此之間的愛心，社團成立的初心就是不希望看到台灣人彼此之間的不信任，不尊重，欺負，欺騙，拉仇恨和聚眾霸凌，台灣最美的風景是人，希望在這個新園地裏，把最美的風景帶到異鄉的每個角落。 版規 （1）不要洗版，除了管理員，每日每人貼文最多三篇 （2）請在提問和發言時不要忘記說「請；謝謝；和對不起」，喜歡的貼文也請按個讚，表達鼓勵 （3）有關宗教政治的貼文，立場可以不同，但絕對禁止互相言語攻擊 （4）社團禁止任何私人之間的商業行為，直銷請止步 （5）管理員有權力刪除任何讓人不舒服和有爭議的貼文留言，刪除不會另外通知和解釋 （6）請勿封鎖管理員，一經發現立刻刪除團員資格，不另外通知 （7）社團禁止隨意張貼外部連結，例如宣傳個人粉絲頁或是網站 （8）團員貼文之後，不可隨意刪除貼文和留言，版內貼文與內容絕對禁止截圖外流 （9）對自己不認同的貼文和留言，請尊重對方，做到不看不發言繞道而行，社團的每個人都有發文發言權，但最終裁決權由管理員決定 （10）為了維護社團和管理員公正立場，不會介入處理團員們之間的糾紛，請團員們自行私下解決 （11）禁止所有募款活動，社團大型版聚需先經過管理員批准 （12）在社團請用繁體中文或是英文發言和貼文 違反版規者，立即刪除團員資格，不會另外通知
                </div>

                 READ THE BELOW: Travelling USA, Backpacking USA, Travel USA, Solo Travel, Budget Travel, Mid-Range Travel, Backpackers, Couple, Tour Travel, USA Tour Travel. THE GROUP is mostly for written posts specific to the destination. POSTS ARE FOR ALL style of travellers – backpackers, budget travellers, mid range, couples, adventure travel and even some luxury travellers. The group is mainly for the DESTINATION, not the style. *ANNOUNCEMENTS: Please check the ‘Announcements’ tab at the top or side of the group. These are for the members benefit. FAQ ANSWERS TOP RECOMMENDATIONS FULL LINKS STOP REPEATED QUESTIONS RECOMMENDATIONS INCLUDE: Best places to stay, tours, insurance, visas, transport and more. WE ONLY collaborate with reputable and highly recommended companies for you to have the OPTION to choose from (with links). PLEASE NOTE these posts may sometimes be in content form and in an advertising format. Please appreciate these recommendations; they are there to help! YOUR POSTS: Approved once per day. Allow 24 hours+. If it’s urgent, contact ADMIN. Please be patient for us to approve posts. WE ALLOW: questions, advice, experiences, images &amp; videos (no tags) and relevant information travel articles. RECOMMENDATIONS, BLOGGERS OR TRAVEL COMPANIES get in touch if it BENEFITS the members. GROUP NO NO’S NO Shared content, self-promotion or unnecessary tags. NO members with fake looking profiles, no display pictures or who have suspiciously joined too many groups. NO abusive members NO spam NO posts about other destinations other than this group. NO un-solicited content or self-promotion blogs WHAT YOU CAN DO TO HELP REPORT Spam, fake profiles, abusive members EMBRACE the recommendations we provide POST your travel photos without tags CONNECT and MEET UP with others PROVIDE sound advice and recommendations CONTACT ADMIN: For travel advice or questions. The group is trying to help, if you disagree that’s your decision and you’re welcome to leave or become inactive at any time. Travellers help travellers and this is what this group is about! Thanks and safe travels! Please DON'T post: • Commercial type posts promoting your business. See below for more info! • Self promotion and Instagram pods. From time to time, we will have official group Instagram pods so we can all grow together! Too many pods start to spam up the feed. • Copy and pasted comments into multiple threads. • Links to or promotions of outside groups. • MLM posts and spammy looking posts will be removed. Traveling on a budget, where to stay, what to do, etc. • Questions and ideas for working while you travel! • Adventure pictures!! If you're on a trip, share it! :) Let's inspire each other to travel more! • Articles, videos, and other cool travel things you find! • Questions about travel, how tor seeking travel advice! If you break the rules, you may be removed without warning or explanation. We want to make sure that this group stays positive, uplifting, helpful, and fun for us all to connect and share in! Thanks so much for sharing your adventures and travel tips here, I love our little growing community!! Please be kind and inspiring in your posts and comments!! This community is a place for all of us travel-minded girls to help each other take on our dreams! :) If you would like to promote your company as a remote opportunity with designated posts within the group, please contact our business development department. 2142889654 dpemberton@inclineme.com If you would like to partner with Kūlana to allow our ambassadors to rep your products or company online, please email kulanaco@inclineme.com Managing a group this size can take a lot of time and effort.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Travelers of the U.S. National Parks
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 There is such beauty in the national parks in the U.S. which many of us never get to witness in person, especially the more remote areas. My goal is to help organize like-minded people who have an interest in experiencing that beauty while sharing it with a few friends. This is an open group whose purpose is to serve as a forum to help organize people in small trips around the country (mostly by means of roadtrips) to explore, hike, camp, and absorb the beauty of the national parks (state parks too). It is very informal, anyone can organize/lead a trip, and at anytime of the year. I hope people will have lots of great experiences and make lots of new friends. Enjoy this networking forum. Please share experiences, wonderful locations you’ve already found or places you want to go. (perhaps soon we can make an international feature).

                 EUROPE 🇪🇺 Travel Community
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 PLEASE READ: We welcome all new members to the "EUROPE Backpacker / Traveler" group. This group, which is operated by Backpacker-Footsteps, exists so that all members can share valuable information to travelers in Europe. Since we always want to support you with your travels around the world, you may visit our website (www.backpacker-footsteps.com) or our FB page for more backpacking details! (http://bit.ly/2pryUnN) Here’s a list of all backpacker FB groups that we are currently running: (http://bit.ly/2pv1g2E) As of today, there are more than 300,000 backpackers and travelers who share their travel experiences in our groups. Join us now and be part of our growing community! Please read our Impressum under this link (http://bit.ly/2qg1L1e), and always read and follow our group’s rules for posting (see details below). Thank you very much! **************Advice and Rules for posting in the “EUROPE Backpacker / Traveler” group************** &gt;&gt; All posts and all links must be in English ONLY. Posts or links in other languages will be removed. &gt;&gt; Please take a moment before you post, and ask yourself if what you're posting will be helpful to all the travelers. &gt;&gt; If you have a lot to share, please don't share it all at once. We only welcome one post a day from any of our members because more than that is a bit too much. &gt;&gt; DO NOT start any heated discussions regarding religion, politics or other subjects that will automatically lead to people getting angry or offended. &gt;&gt; DO NOT use abusive or threatening language when replying to posts/comments. If you do not like the post, you can always ignore it; however, if the post is deemed inappropriate, you may report it to the admins by tagging them in the comments section. &gt;&gt; NO HATE SPEECH. Members are to be respected and should be helpful to one another. &gt;&gt; DO NOT promote your business. You will get a friendly warning if you post several times per day, and if you keep breaking the rule, we will have to delete/ban you from the page (this rule applies to members trying to sell personal belongings too). &gt;&gt; THIS IS NOT THE PLACE TO PROMOTE YOUR BLOG OR GROUP. If you want to post about your travel, send us a message and we will post it for you. &gt;&gt; DO NOT post ads selling smartphones in bulk, ads offering loans, investment etc. &gt;&gt; NO SURVEYS, NO ASKING FOR CASH* DONATIONS POSTS, NO PERSONAL ATTACK ON GROUPS/INDIVIDUALS OR SCAM WARNINGS &gt;&gt; DO NOT post a link without any text or explanation. It will be deleted. &gt;&gt; DO NOT post any advertising or any affiliated marketing links wherein you get to earn a credit every time an individual clicks through it. &gt;&gt; Join this group only if you are a person that has an actual Facebook profile. &gt;&gt; Always use the search box to look for hostels or accommodations, or you may also try using Trip Advisor or Hostelworld prior asking the group. Please always follow the rules, keep a good tone and enjoy the group.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Women Who Travel
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Conde Nast Traveler's Women Who Travel group, a place where all self-identifying female travel lovers can join in conversation about what it means to travel as a woman today. Community Guidelines: DO engage with the community, share and comment on posts, and tag your friends! DO ask questions and give answers to other group members—but please be respectful of our differing opinions on the world. DO stay on topic: This is a group about travel, so let's talk all things travel! DO use the ‘search’ bar on the left before asking for travel tips: duplicate threads may be deleted! DO lift other women up––we encourage positivity! NO spam. NO advertisements: all posts advertising items for sale, personal businesses, and travel agencies will be deleted and posters will be removed.* NO soliciting. NO hate speech: Bullying other group members will not be tolerated and offenders will be removed from the group. Harassment of a group moderator or member, even outside of the group, will lead to being blocked. If you experience bullying, please contact Facebook directly. *The ONLY two exceptions to no advertisements: 1. As Condé Nast Traveler, the admin account for this group, we will sometimes post about Women Who Travel meetups, trips, and podcast episodes. We have developed these for this group, and will share them here. 2.) There are three dedicated threads in this group that will act as our community bulletin boards. One is for sharing volunteer opportunities, one is for sharing your social media handles (personal only), and one is for sharing your travel blogs (travel only, please!). These are the only places you may promote these items in the group. Use the search bar to locate them. Please help us keep this space safe: report any posts that violate these community guidelines using the 'report' feature alongside comments and posts. Direct messages to moderators will not be responded to. If you start a thread, you will always have the power to turn off comments, hide responses, and delete the post if need be. If something violates Facebook's community guidelines, you should report posts directly to Facebook. (Please keep in mind that the moderators are only online during normal business hours from 10am-5pm EST, Monday-Friday. Please use self-moderating tips above during on and off hours.) Continue the conversation with us every week on our Women Who Travel Podcast, hosted by moderators Meredith and Lale: https://itunes.apple.com/us/podcast/women-who-travel/id1321118314?mt=2 Read more stories about female travelers on our site: http://cntrvlr.co/5lkBb8z By joining this group, you agree to these community guidelines.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 On the Road in Mexico
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 OTRIM is a great place to talk about road travel in Mexico - the good, the bad and the fun! People are expected to use common sense when posting, and show RESPECT for others; i.e. No attacking members, name calling, use of the “F-word,” racism, etc. POSTING OF SALES, RENTALS AND SERVICES ARE ALLOWED EVERY SUNDAY ONLY. All posts on other days will be deleted. Absolutely no multi-level marketing, money “loaning” or other “financial,” or GoFundMe posts. No “Help Wanted” unless it is a LOCAL, PHYSICAL business, and we vet the post. Repeated offenders will be blocked. This does not mean that if a person asks question, one cannot be referred to other sites that have an answer, but stand-alone post promotions of service-related websites or persons will be limited to SUNDAYS ONLY. We do NOT ALLOW people recommending others to BREAK THE LAW in Mexico, i.e. bring a gun for protection – and is ILLEGAL, as is paying mordida (bribes). Both are against Federal laws of Mexico. This does not stop people from discussing some common concerns that involve breaking the law, i.e. bribery of traffic police officers. This is a very controversial subject with many points of view. Discussion of this subject is education for both long term Mexican travelers and new ones. NO POLITICAL DISCUSSIONS OTHER THAN OF MEXICO are allowed, nor any topics that are politically divisive, or pertain to other countries. No links that lead to political commentary. NO COMPARISONS of Mexico vs the US, Canada, etc. Those posts get radical quickly and lead to virtual fist-fights. We are not concerned with the laws or customs in those, except for border crossings. NO discussion of immigrants, legal or otherwise, derogatory, or sensationalist statements of the same. INFORMATION PERTINENT TO TRAVELERS or immigrants from other countries (insurance “back home”, how to register for Absentee Ballots, etc) IS allowed. ANYONE WHO BLOCKS ANY ADMIN WILL BE OUSTED &amp; BLOCKED FROM OTRIM. The reason we have instated rules is to try and keep peace among 41,500+ members, as well as our own sanity. We try to keep this a positive group, focused on travel within Mexico. Negative posts and comments made simply to complain may be removed. Note: All photos posted on in this group may be used for non-commercial publication in the Sol Mexico News. Thank you, ~Admin
                </div>

Please join with a real personal account. - No commercial advertising. Tips and useful information about Cancun is allowed, but please avoid advertising. Only admins have the authorization to post advertising when they feel it would be helpful. - No posting of external websites or Facebook pages purely to drive traffic. By all means post links to relevant articles or pages, but normally these will not be a site/page you have a direct interest in. - No personal attacks, hostility, vulgarity or racist, homophobic and sexist comments. - Threads, posts and photos should be related to issues relating to Cancun. No off topic memes, foreign sports, foreign politics etc. - English is the primary language of the group. If you start a thread in Spanish please provide an English translation. - Photos should be your own, have the consent of the people in them and comply with Facebook Community standards. Admin decisions are final and not open to debate.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Come Visit My Philippines
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 COME VISIT MY PHILIPPINES ~ How we started.... "Believe in the beauty of your country....you deserve a visit from the world!" ~ Tourism Secretary Ramon Jimenez Jr. Moved and inspired by an article on Ramon Jimenez, Bessie Badilla and friends started posting photographs they took in the Philippines on their Facebook accounts. They wanted to show the world they "believe in the beauty of their country," and somehow hoped they would make a difference....their posted images caught on and the threads began to grow! Fascinated by the positive response from numerous Facebook users, another friend Francois Medina decided that they should start a Facebook page for Filipinos who feel the same way....they would start a new Philippine Tourism campaign by posting photos of their beautiful country and use the tag- phrase, "COME VISIT MY PHILIPPINES!" It was targeted to get the attention of the Filipinos on Facebook! If every one of the 25 Million Filipinos on Facebook would invite ONE friend to visit the Philippines, then Philippine tourism would get the boost it needs! The group "COME VISIT MY PHILIPPINES" is open to all who BELIEVE in the beauty of the Philippines. Members are free to post photos of their favorite resort, fiesta, food, landscape, scenery, vacation spot, beach, landmarks etc of the Philippines. The group was formed on Sunday, September 25, 2011 at 12 noon....24 hours later, the group had 3,500 members and still growing! Due to the overwhelming number of member requests, the group invited more friends to be administrators. They wanted to have a 24/7 watch so every member request is accepted at any time of the day. We ALL Believe in PINOY POWER! MABUHAY ang PILIPINO!

                 The Solo Female Traveler Network
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome Solo Female Travelers! www.thesolofemaletravelernetwork.com I have started this group, because in my travels I have found a need for more support for the ladies who are braving the world on their own. Find us on INSTAGRAM! @SoloFemaleTravel #SoFeTravel With your help, I want to create a space for all female travelers to be able to come for not just travel advice, but also to ask if that local was being creepy or cultural, get support for homesickness, show off the amazing photos from your last trip, tell stories, and whatever is on your mind. *I hope this group will be encouragement to watch out for each other online, on the road, at home, and always. * Rules: DO NOT PROMOTE YOUR BLOG. No one wants a page full of self promotion, and I don't have time to send friendly reminders to everyone, so just don't do it. I will delete it. This includes articles, instagrams, etc. Instead join our digital nomad group! https://www.facebook.com/groups/138860990111757/ NO LOOKING FOR TRAVEL BUDDIES to plan a trip with. If you are going somewhere and want to see if anyone is there to meet, cool! If you are not traveling otherwise, no looking for people to plan, commit to, and go on a trip with. It's dangerous and not in the spirit of solo travel. Instead join our sister group specifically for meet ups! https://m.facebook.com/groups/291987397956416 NO LOOKING OR OFFERING FREE ACCOM Instead, join our sister group for this! https://www.facebook.com/groups/136753883609549/ COMMENTS THAT OFFEND WILL BE DELETED without explanation. In most cases YOU WILL DELETED for meanness, racism, name calling, cyber bullying, etc. If you don't help cultivate a space of community, inspiration, and support then you don't belong here. DO YOUR RESEARCH BEFORE POSTING. We are here as support, not to plan your trip. In most cases, posts like "I am going to X city. What do you recommend?" will be deleted. Not because we don't love talking travel (obviously), but because these clog up the feed, and let's face it, are a little lazy. Do your research and ask us specific questions that you can't find in a Google search. :) Be open. Be kind. Be genuine. Ladies only. Photos encouraged.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Travel Community
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This travel community is a place for like-minded people to engage with others that love to discuss travel. GUIDELINES: ____________ 1. NO advertising or selling anything on this page: ► NO external links to groups/FB pages/websites/businesses with an aim of advertising ► NO spamming ► DO NOT privately DM anyone unsolicited to promote ANYTHING whatsoever. ► 1st OFFENSE: you will be removed from the group 2. DO NOT go live via video in the group without asking an admin first. 3. Please DO: ► Share uploaded pictures &amp; videos, experiences, tips, &amp; questions for all members to learn from. This is your community. Jump in and engage often! ► Report harassment and spamming. Click the “report to admin” and admins will assist ASAP. ► Use the search bar before asking a question – it’s located at the top of the group page. This avoids multiple posts about the same topic &amp; is also often a quicker way to get an answer to your question. ► Be as specific as possible with your questions. No “I’m going to Hawaii. Where should I eat?” or “I’m visiting Amsterdam, where should I stay?” That’s what Google is for. Include your preferences, age group(s) of travelers, budget, etc. 4. Photos/videos: ► Post your own photos or give credit ► Include the location(s) ► NO photos of children unless part of your travel group ► If posting with wildlife, include specific location (zoo, sanctuary, reserve, etc.) ► Admins have final say on approval for any photo/video 4. Etiquette: Be courteous &amp; respectful. This isn’t a place to share your political views or bully someone with a different opinion. If you disagree, act like an adult and either don’t respond or kindly disagree and move on. We MUST value each other’s input in this community! 5. Travel agents and marketers: ► DO NOT post/comment to promote your travel agency and/or company. ► DO NOT privately DM group members unsolicited. ► DO NOT leave your contact info or promotional campaign info in any comments. You may provide such information ONLY when specifically asked for your direct contact info. 6. Bloggers/Media/Influencers: ► You may share uploaded photos &amp; videos from your travels. ► NO linking to your website/blog or social media channels. ► If someone comments asking for more info, you can THEN reply with a link in the comments. 7. DO NOT ask for or share medical advice. Medical professionals should be consulted outside of this group. 8. NO posts asking for travel companions. 9. Any content or a member disrupting the community can be removed without any communication on the personal discretion of the admin of the group. 10. DO NOT post questions about your Scott’s Cheap Flights account. Please email support@scottscheapflights.com 11. See something negative report it. 12. Admins observe the right to decline topics and turn off comments or delete posts. 
                </div>

                 PLEASE READ: We welcome to the "Thailand, Cambodia, Laos and Vietnam Backpacker / Traveler" group. This group, which is operated by Backpacker-Footsteps. Join us now and be part of our growing community! Post and comment ONLY in English language or if you want to post in your native languages you MUST have the English version too or the post will be removed. 2. DO NOT talk about sex, religion, politics or Unethical Animal Tourism (Elephant riding, Tiger cuddling, swimming with whalesharks etc) and whatever is not about Thailand, Cambodia, Laos and Vietnam, this includes any country not mentioned. See the LIST of other COUNTRIES GROUPS above. 3. DO NOT use abusive or threatening language when replying to posts/comments. If you do not like the post you can ignore it and if it's inappropriate you can report to the admins. 4. NO HATE SPEECH, members are to be respectful and helpful to the others. 5. DO NOT promote your business, website, blog, facebook page, Instagram, Youtube or other groups, NO LIVE STREAM without permission: This is the only friendly warning you will get if you keep breaking the rule we will ban you from the page. [ this includes unsolicited contact per private message]. 6. Every post that will be considered as spam will be immediately deleted and the user will be immediately banned from the group. 7. DO NOT post a link without any text or explanation and nothing with personal data of anyone. It will be deleted. 8. DO NOT ask stupid questions. We reserve the right to delete any post which WE do not think belongs in the group 9. Please try to use the search box to search if somebody has already opened a threat about what you looking for or, if somebody already asked the question you got in your mind. 10. *NO SURVEYS, NO ASKING FOR CASH* DONATIONS POSTS FOLLOWERS OR SUBSCRIBERS, NO PERSONAL ATTACKS ON GROUPS/INDIVIDUALS OR SCAM WARNINGS 11.Do NOT post any advertising that relate your own profit such as hotel linkor any other affiliate link. Password: EpicTravelShow 12. If you do want to advertise in this group and have a mutually beneficial offer please contact Eugene Reimer 13. If you are a Blogger or Youtuber and are interested in collaborating with us please contact Jonny Hamburg

JOIN NOW!, ✈️ WHO ARE WE? ✈️ Hi! My name is Julie, I'm a flight attendant with American Airlines. I love to travel and share new ideas with fellow colleagues. Here is a place where you can share trips, tips and ideas about the more interesting, fun and adventurous vacations you have been on for our fellow fAAmily to read about. Please feel free to post news of your experiences, fun pictures and videos, and let us know where and how you booked your adventure. AA Travel Adventures is a global community of active and enthusiastic American Airline employees (retired and inactive AA employees are welcome as well). This is a safe and FUN place to connect with American Airline friends - where you can share your travel stories, and discover and share resources for inside scoops on everything employee travel and adventure. ~ IMPORTANT: When requesting to join this group you must answer the questions in order for me to verify you. It takes me a long time to verify each member please help me by doing this thank you ~ ✈️ GROUP RULES ✈️ Our #1 rule is to help make this a friendly and fun online environment for all your new American Airline friends here at AA Non Rev Travel Adventures! As we start to grow our community here are our basic guidelines to follow: • Posts that go against our guidelines will be removed (often without warning) • All posts must be travel focused, and all comments on posts should be relevant to the posted discussion. • RESPECT is REQUIRED in ALL exchanges between members. • ZERO TOLERANCE for disrespecting or degrading any race, religion, culture, sexual orientation, gender, identity, etc. • ZERO TOLERANCE for bullying, attacking, or escalating fights. • DO NOT DISRESPECT OR BLOCK the admin or any of the moderators. • Spam is not allowed on the main feed - If spam links are not removed, your post might be deleted • AA Travel Adventures is for anyone who is an employee, retiree, family member or Spouse of an American Airlines (Mesa, Envoy and Eagle too). NO SCREEN SHOTS PLEASE it is against company policy to post screen shots of non rev lists or from Jet net thank you DISCLAIMER ~ The views reflected on this page do not reflect the corporation and each individual is responsible for the consequences of what they put in writing.

                 Disneyland will never be completed. It will continue to grow as long as there is imagination left in the world. Walt Disney Description I created this page for all Disneyland Addicts! We all love Disney, no matter how old you are! We are young at heart! The DLA page is for those that are addicted to Disney, all things big and small! This includes sharing our excitement of our upcoming trips, getting advice, sharing our favorite Disney photos or sharing information of the latest and greatest that is happening at Disneyland! This is DLA’s focus. Our focus is also why Disneyland is so special to us and all DLA should keep those memories in mind when participating on the DLA page. Anything outside of these parameters need to be reported to one of the Admins to keep the page fun and friendly. Sarah McClure is our go to gal for all things travel! She is a supervisory agent with an Authorized Disney Vacation Planner agency, Wishes Family Travel. She also books Good Neighbor Hotels and anything else you are looking to do she can help! And!!! Her services are free! So send her a PM if you are thinking of booking! :) No other travel agent solicitations allowed. We love seeing all your Disney creations and if you have a platform to sell them that is awesome! We will offer a post offering vendors the opportunity to share links to their shops. Please only post a link to your shop in the comments of these threads. From there your discussion with people about your product will need to take place in a private message. NO SOLICITATION ON THE GROUP WALL. PLEASE FOLLOW GUIDELINES ABOVE. Feeding into those that are soliciting or causing issues on our page is also NOT acceptable Disney behavior and can lead to removal from the group as well. Please do not converse with those soliciting or spamming. PLEASE report the person to one of the Admins and DELETE the post from your timeline. Let's keep the posts fun and friendly. Enjoy!! Now let's get down to Disney Magic! :) ºoº ºoº ºoº ºoº ºoº Founded August 23rd, 2014

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Hawaii Travel Tips 🇦🇺🏝
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Aloha! This is a group for Australians, Americans, and travellers from around the world planning to visit Hawaii! 🤙 Anyone is welcome to join, and please share any information that has helped you save money or enhance your experience in Hawaii! 😎🤙 There are plenty of amazing things to do, places to eat, and beautiful properties to stay at that can be had at a reasonable price. Every dollar you save is a little more ALOHA you are able to experience :-) We will also be sharing helpful tips we have learned over the years as well as great deals on some of our favorite Happy Hours, Hotels, and Shopping! Please feel free to ask the community any questions about your holiday plans to Hawaii, and please be respectful of other peoples opinions and posts. Mahalo, The Hawaii Travel Tips Team!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Black Travel Movement
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Black Travel Movement is a community of friends and family who share an interest in cultivating new friendships and epic experiences through international worldwide travel. As a member of the BTM family you have a connection to a wide range of new and seasoned travelers who are anxious to join and share travel experiences. Although we are a new online community many of our members have decades of experience as world-class travelers. We also have experienced travel professional who are committed to helping create and organize the best values on the market for our travel and vacation experiences. We welcome members to share their photos, videos, and stories as they travel the globe and create new friendships and memories. Please invite your crew, your friends, and your family to join our group. ** Rules for Posting to the BTM Group Page. (These rules are also listed in the group files) Here are the rules and suggestions for posting to the group: 1. Please post your travel photos and share interesting stories and experiences. 2. Feel free to ask questions or start a discussion related to travel and travel experiences. Please use hashtags to help with searches. 3. PLEASE DO NOT POST ANYTHING NOT RELATED TO TRAVEL. 4. Please do not post anything that promotes a business or non BTM trips or events 5. Please do not post anything related to MLM and network marketing opportunities. You will be removed and blocked. 6. Please do not post anything related to travel clubs or discount cards. 7. Please do not post any offers or free giveaways 8. Please do a search in the group before asking for advice or recommendations. Chances are your question has already been asked and answered. 9. Please do not post anything that request members to email or call you. 10. Please do not post links to other Facebook pages or groups, Instagram pages, or Twitter pages. 11. Please do not post pictures with "You Should Be Here" signs. 12. Please do not post introductions resembling dating page bios 13. If your pictures are more about you than the destination, location, or experience please post them to your personal page. 14. Please do not post sexually suggestive bikini and bathing suit pictures (backshots) 15. Please be respectful of others and refrain from posting inappropriate language or images. 16. BTM reserves the right to use any picture posted to the group page for display, marketing and/or promotion on the group page, our Instagram page, Twitter page, or website. 17. Please do not make uninvited advances toward other members of the group. 18. Please do not make comments or post that could be construed as "Travel Shaming". 19. Travel agents may reply to request for "travel agents" 20. Each of these rules apply to comment threads and inboxes ** Violating any of the posting rules is grounds for removal from the group** Thank you and welcome to the BTM Family Reggie Cummings Founder Black Travel Movement

More: www.seeyouiniran.org Join us by: 1. Asking your non-Iranian and first/second generation Iranian friends who have visited Iran to post a paragraph about their experience with some pictures. 2. Adding potential visitors who have expressed interest in visiting Iran. 3. Adding potential hosts and travel companions in Iran.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 A Year of Travel
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Can you visit 12 new places you've never been, meet someone new and learn about their life? Visiting 12 new places is a lot -- it's one new place every month. The places don't need to be far away. A half-hour drive, bus or train ride to meet people in a community you don't normally interact with counts. A road trip could be a way to meet people in 5-10 different places in a week or less. And even if you don't visit 12 new places, meeting people in any new community can be a meaningful experience. This is a group for all of us to share stories of our adventures traveling to new places and meeting new people with different perspectives.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 VIKING RIVER &amp; OCEAN CRUISES FRIENDS
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 THIS IS NOT A COMPANY OR TRAVEL AGENT RUN GROUP! OVERVIEW This group's purpose is to share our experiences and recommendations with other travelers about Viking Cruises. Friendly behavior to other group members is expected. Please be kind to each other, post pictures, ask questions, share knowledge, enjoy the group and HAVE SOME FUN! The group has the word FRIENDS in the title for two reasons. We are friends of Viking Cruises and are each other’s friends. The is the place to share your joy of traveling with Viking. And to get help to find ways to enjoy it even more. CIVILITY EXPECTED Disagreeing is just fine, BUT trading insults is most certainly not. Admins will do their best to maintain civility in the group, but it is each member’s responsibility to stay civil in the first place. If a post starts generating insulting comments, comments on that post will be turn off or the post itself will be deleted. Comments may also be turned off when the discussion becomes too repetitive. TRAVEL AGENTS/AGENCIES If you are a travel agent, you are NOT allowed to post or send messages to group members soliciting business. Also the naming travel agents or agencies by group members is not allowed. Offers or request to PM the names to get around the rules are also not allowed. Such posts will be deleted. Discussing the pros and cons of booking directly with Viking vs. using a TA is fine. SPAMMING EVENTS Clicking "Going" on multiple events that you are not booked on will cause a member to be blocked from the group. DISCUSSIONS ABOUT RULES Our group rules are simple. Just follow them. Posts discussing the rules and rule administration are not appropriate. Such posts will be removed or have their comments closed. People come here to discuss Viking not to discuss our easy to follow rules. MARITIME ACCIDENT POSTS Posts for or including links to maritime Incidents are serious, but they do not have a place in our group for a few key reasons , namely: - they are international news and can easily be googled to find the info - they create conditions for speculative comments with people guessing without all the facts on who to blame - we are not experts but even if there are experts our group this is not the place for such a discussion. So... Such posts will be deleted without prior notice. VIKING EMPLOYEES If you work for Viking, you are very welcome here. We appreciate your help and advice. If you are looking for a job, this is not the right place. Instead, please go to the official Viking page to apply your CV: https://www.vikingcareers.com OFF TOPIC POSTS Finally a note that only admins can post off topic posts. Some examples of off topic posts would be giving or asking for medical advice or a discussion that solely focuses on another cruise line. Examples of things on topic would be a comparison of Viking versus some other line or of a private excursion done during, before or after a Viking cruise.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome all solo female travelers over 40! This group is a sub-group of The Solo Female Traveler Network, specifically for connecting solo female travelers who are over 40 and are braving the world on their own. This group is to connect with one another as experienced, world-wise solo female travelers. Ask questions about travel specifically for this crowd.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Learn to unlock the power of credit card, hotel, and airline points/miles to travel the world on any budget! Welcome to Award Travel 101, the original Facebook community created for miles and points enthusiasts. Our goal is to help you learn how to maximize your travel rewards, no matter your destination or budget. Our members visit their friends and family, explore new destinations, and experience previously imagined adventures for pennies on the dollar. Join us for regular segments that sharpen your loyalty program knowledge and teach new tips: #DecisionMonday - Get advice on what credit card you should get next. #StackIt - Just looking to up your monthly earnings by using a double-, triple-, or even quadruple-stack on a single purchase? We search for ways to improve your earnings. ##TacoTuesdayQA - Each Tuesday, ask your travel-related questions in a rapid-fire Q+A chat with our moderators. #VirtualVisits - Travel advice for the destinations you want to know about. #DecisionThursday - Same as Monday. So many questions we have to do it twice a week! #BragoftheWeek - Shout Out to the whole group how you used miles and points for that awesome trip! #WeekendBurn - All weekend long, ask your questions about booking award flights and be sure to help out other members when you can. #ShareYourSnapSunday - Got an amazing shot on your last trip? Share your best photos with the whole group here! In addition to those scheduled weekly threads, stop by anytime to see a variety of member submitted posts throughout each day. You never know what you may learn or how you may be able to help someone out. We look forward to you joining the discussion on the latest news and strategies to help you earn and redeem your points and miles for the best possible value. We're passionate about getting every last penny from those hard-earned rewards. Please be sure to read the pinned announcement for helpful tools to get you started on your journey to see the world courtesy of points and miles. - Toni, John, &amp; Joe Community Managers, Award Travel 101 — Follow us on Twitter and Instagram - @AwardTravel101 — Subscribe to our Youtube Channel where you can view replays of our live videos and see some awesome clips of our travels - https://Award.Travel/youtube

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 NOMADS - a life of alternative travel
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Here is an overview of the group GUIDELINES. NOMADS' PHILOSOPHY - This group is for ideas and discussions about long-term, low-impact, low budget, mindful life on the road. This is NOT a general travel group. We will always support alternative ways of life and travel, that encourage active engagement with the world to create positive change. We value travels without flying and moneyless exchanges between people. ... Example of Topics we DO encourage: ● interesting mindful hitchhiking stories ● overland/ low impact travel i.e. on bicycle, walking etc. ● sustainable/carbon-neutral nomadism ● urban / stealth / wild camping / sleeping on the streets / squatting ● hospitality exchanges ● living in/with a tent / hammock/ bivy / tarp ● dumpster diving ● meaningful moneyless volunteering exchanges ● busking / street performance ● moneyless journey ● rubber-tramping (living and travelling in a vehicle, full-time) ● commune/co-operative/eco-village/community life ● traveling with a disability, chronic illness / mental illness ● alternative and renewable energy on the road ● LGBTIQ+ travel - safety discussions and tips ● ethical traveling: environmental friendly and cruelty free traveling ... Do NOT post: ● Questions asking how to travel from A to B ● Any posts mentioning flying ● Questions asking cheaper air tickets or bus tickets ● Questions asking cheap hostels or the cheapest places to stay ● Any selling posts ● Any fundraising ● Spam/Trolling ● Room / house renting. There are other websites for this ● Competitions: “Please like / vote this picture” ● Any polls, surveys or fee-based events. ● Your travel related blog repetitively. Exceptions will be made at admin discretion of the content is strongly aligned with our values - though this is non-negotiable. ● Links without relevant captions. ● Comments only to follow the post. There is an option to get notifications without writing any comment on a post. Top right corner of the post -&gt; pull down menu -&gt; turn ON notifications. ... Please read the full version on this link before posting: https://docs.google.com/document/d/1b7IGgScejedNV6WQGvkRJYqnE0tdkUwN9flLfTCn4gM/edit Thanks for reading and welcome to our group! FB page - FB.com/nomadslifeofcheapfreetravel

                 Golden Age Of Travel 1830-1955
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Golden Age of Travel is often described as the period between the 1830s to the early 1950s (excluding the two world wars). Travel was by ships, trains, planes, automobiles, etc. Accommodations were luxurious. Posts should relate to the Golden Age of Travel 1830-1955: where vacationers went, what they saw, or how they got there. Posters, old photos (or modern, if they depict interesting passenger transportation or beautiful old buildings, such as castles), advertisements, etc. if your post was deleted it may mean that it was too far outside the theme.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Lonely Planet Travellers Community! We hope that you’re familiar with our travel resources like our destination guide books, apps, and our website. Our collective goal is to keep you up to date with all the travel news and information, as well as tips and tricks to aid in your travels from the most well known destinations to hidden corners around the world. You’ll also have exclusive and early bird access to new launches, and access to our Q/A from our experts. As a member, you’ll find a community of passionate like-minded travellers who are generous with their collective knowledge and share your enthusiasm for exploring the world. We invite you to share your travel tips, personal stories, travel reviews, and photos from your travel adventures. Feel free to add your opinions or tips to one of our weekly threads, or help out your fellow travellers by providing value and insights. We may use your questions in editorial posts so we can share the knowledge. While we understand that we have people from all backgrounds here, we want to make sure that our conversations are more advanced than beginner. Based on the needs of the community, you’ll find that we may create new hubs to allow for more nuanced conversations more freely. Community Rules &amp; Guidelines: This group is a place to have real time conversation about travel. All posts must be relevant, and respectful to all users of the forum. Any posts containing explicit language, graphic violence, sexually explicit material, or calls for boycott of a business will be promptly removed along with the member who posted it. We also do not support any illegal activities or posting other member’s private information. This is a self-promotion free zone, so all posts in this group must not have any intent to advertise or profit. Please refrain from contacting members of this group via private messenger as that will also result in a ban. We believe responsible travel is a force for good… now more so than ever it's important to appreciate the variety of cultures, people and places that make our world so incredibly diverse. We hope you’ll find all the inspiration, tips and advice you’re looking for when it comes to exploring the world in this group, however near or far your adventure may be. 
                </div>
               </div>

                 Black Folks Travel Too!ᵀᴹ
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Black people have always been travelers, but we don't always see that reflected in the mainstream media. We created this forum as a place to share travel photos, videos, information, questions and recommendations. Whether you've traveled internationally, domestically or are just discovering the treasures near your home, please share and participate. POSTING RULES 1. Posts must be travel related. 2. Posts cannot promote any personal businesses or services. 3. No advertising of MLM or network marketing opportunities. 4. No advertising of non BFTT trips or events. Only BFTT group events are allowed to be posted on the page. 5. Please do not post links to other Facebook groups or travel pages. 6. No hashtags to travel websites, products or services. 7. Please do not post requests for travel partners to join you on a trip. 8. A post will not be put up if it duplicates another post that has been previously submitted the same day. Our goal is to keep fresh content, without being repetitive. 9. Posts will not be approved if admins cannot view the post. Sometimes members submit posts that can only be seen by their FB friends, so the submission will say…”CONTENT NOT AVAILABLE”. 10. There is a list of “Popular Topics” at the top of the page so be sure to check that list if you’re looking for information about a particular destination or subject. If you add a post please be sure to tag it with one of those topics. It’s a great resource. 11. The focus of this group is to promote travel and destinations, so if your pictures or videos are more about you than the destination, location, or experience please post them to your personal page. 12. Rules apply to posts and comments and are also listed in the Group Files. Violating any of the posting rules is grounds for removal from the group. BFTT is a positive community, a place to share and request travel information. Although there will be differences of opinion and/or disagreements, we can disagree without being disagreeable. Comments that harass, insult or demean other group members will be removed and the person who posted the comment will be removed. Do not post public comments requesting contacts for business, or send private messages to group members soliciting for business. You will be removed.

(NSFW photos, however, are subject to removal.) - Please use the SEARCH bar before posting. - This group is for members who are A)members of the main GLT group and B) identify as women. If you meet someone outside of the group - you will be removed from this group and we wish you well in your future endeavors! See the list below: Be Respectful We all have opinions. There are lots of them that we want to share and we should, as long as we understand that differing opinions should not turn into a bout of intentional attacks. We ask that you keep an open mind and monitor the language you use during interactions. Be Beautiful We already know you’re beautiful on the outside but we’re looking for that inner beauty in this case. True beauty showcases itself in class and grace. Share your beauty by extending compliments about someone else’s. Being beautiful is not gender specific. Be Wise Sometimes things don’t go as well as we would have expected. Before things go left, know when to go right. Ask an administrator for assistance if you’re in need of conflict mediation. Be Alert Be alert in a good way, not an alarming one. This group promotes positivity and active engagement. Participate as often as you can. You never know where future “Bae” may pop up in conversation. Be Warned Violation of the group rules will prompt removal and blocking. That is never our goal but we will not hesitate in removing offenders from an environment that we want to protect from hostility. Solicitation is PROHIBITED in the group unless otherwise allowed in a specific post. Group trip recruitment is also prohibited. Violation of the above stated policies may result in immediate termination without warning.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Travel Meet Ups - The Solo Female Traveler Network
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome all Solo Female Travelers! This group is a sub-group of The Solo Female Traveler Network, specifically for connecting solo gals on the road and meeting fellow solo female traveling locals for drinks or dinner while your in their hometown. This group works the more people we have here, so invite your friends! These are examples of the types of posts allowed in this group: -"I am in Rome! Who wants to meet for vino?" -"I am going to Barcelona in a week. Anyone want to split a hotel room?" -"I have an extra ticket for a helicopter ride. Anyone in Maui now and want to join me?" Here is what is NOT allowed: -SELF PROMO - your post will be deleted and you will be removed without warning -nastiness - name calling, cruelness, and trolling are not tolerated Don't forget to use the SEARCH BAR to see if anyone has already posted that they are in your city! If you haven't already, check out or main group: https://www.facebook.com/groups/thesolofemaletravelernetwork/ And our sister group: https://www.facebook.com/groups/136753883609549/ **Please understand that there is risk in meeting strangers from FB. We do our best to screen our members, but fake profiles and bad people do exist. Just remember that while most of the time people are good, you still need to be smart and careful.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 We're Going to Disney World - Travel Tips and Planning
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Planning a Disney vacation &amp; looking for tips to make the most out of your visit or have info you'd like to share? You've come to the right place! Thanks for joining us to share travel tips and info on our all time favorite vacation destination, Walt Disney World. We want this page to be filled with fun tidbits and helpful information. This page is sponsored by Jen Grandmaison and Ashley Pierce. We are agents from Magic Plus Travel, an Earmarked agency, that specialize in planning Walt Disney World travel, or any Disney Destination. If you have any questions about booking a Disney vacation just contact your preferred agent and we would be happy to provide you a no obligation quote for personalized travel planning and services at no additional cost to you when you book your onsite resort reservation with us. Offsite resort accomodation assistance may also be available as well as customized planning fees for those that want a full level of service but have already secured their reservations elsewhere. You can reach us by email at jen.grandmaison@magicplustravel.com or ashley@magicplustravel.com or by sending us a message on our business pages. Please note that we are not employees of the Walt Disney Travel Company. In order to keep the integrity of the page there are a few things that you need to know. No outside solicitation will be allowed. Soliciting for another agent will be cause for removal from the group. An agent who solicts for themselves will be removed and banned. It doesn't lend anything to your professional credibility to solicit on a page run by another agent or agency. Do not private message members offering products or services. We do not want our members being bombarded with requests by TA's or any other person who sells goods or services. They will seek out the help of an agent or vendor if they need it. So, if you are being solicited from any agents or other member for any reason that you did not initiate, please let us know so that we can address it. Occassionaly we may approve vendor posts and those members must request permission to post prior to doing so. Last but not least, be respectful to one another. It is OK to disagree with someone but do it tactfully. Anyone trying to be argumentative or posting rude/harassing comments will be removed immediately. No vulgar language, name calling or political posts/comments allowed. We reserve the right to remove or ban any member if in violation of these rules. Do not engage in negative banter with someone even if they have been rude to you because you will just get yourself banned as well. The best thing to do is to report any comments or posts that violate the rules and we will handle them as we see fit. We want to keep the magic of Disney on the feed, not bog it down with people arguing or commenting in any way that is less than magical. Thanks for making this one of the fastest growing and best planning groups out there!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Traveling to Italy
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ****PLEASE READ BEFORE JOINING - YOU MUST ANSWER ALL OF THE QUESTIONS BEFORE WE WILL APPROVE YOU. WE WILL NOT APPROVE ANYONE WHO DOES NOT ANSWER ALL THE QUESTIONS.** PLEASE DO NOT SEND ME A FRIEND REQUEST TO JOIN THE GROUP. I started this group so people could share information and experiences/photos on their travels to Italy, and so people who are planning to go can ask questions and get recommendations. RULES: 1. Tour operators, business owners, anyone who provides an Italy travel-related service, etc are all welcome to post in the group. Please just do not spam the page. You must add your info to the pinned post at the top of the page. This is where people will go who are looking for your types of services. Do NOT ask people to PM you for more information. Guide them to the pinned post with the file for travel services. You are welcome to suggest/recommend your services and those of others, WHEN SPECIFICALLY ASKED about your business. WE have to approve posts and will not approve constant spam. We will remove posts, without notice, that break the rules. Repeated refusal to follow this rule may result in being removed from the group without notice. If you want to advertise, please join our sister group, Traveling to Italy - Italy Makers. We are not responsible for any negative experiences anyone may have due to a recommendation here. Everyone else, please use your best judgment when choosing a service from this group. 2. Be Respectful. When someone asks a question, if you can't answer it respectfully, then move along. If someone asks about a group tour, do not tell them not to take a group tour if that's not what they asked. Do not suggest changing their tour, especially if it’s days away. Simply answer the question or move on. 3. NO spam. We will not approve these posts. 4. Please caption your photos with the location. We all want to know the location of your beautiful photos that we should be jealous of! 5. Before asking a question check the files and make use of the search bar located at the top of the group page. This avoids multiple posts about the same topic. It's also a quick way to get an answer to your travel question as it may have already been answered by someone in the community. Repetitive posts will not be approved. If you have questions, please send me a PM. Remember, this is YOUR page. If there is something you don't like, please let me know. Something you want included, also, just let me know. ***Click on the files tab for recommendations from fellow travelers and other great info, including a file for people traveling to Italy and looking for a travel partner or looking to meet up with someone.*** Group Admins: Julie Busa - Creator and Admin. Suzanne Mangini - Admin. Carmel Rose Williams - Admin. Cheryl Davis Hall - Admin.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Carnival Cruise Friends
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 **Welcome, Please take a moment to read the following: Carnival Cruise Friends is a place to come for all things cruise related. Please feel free to share all thoughts, reviews, etc. openly-the good, bad, and ugly. Since our overall desire is to make our cruises the best experience possible, we welcome all comments. As adults we understand that opinions will differ at times, and so we agree to disagree. We are a friendly group. We do not allow any foul language or use other offensive words, you may be muted or removed right away. This includes memes that don't add to the conversation, and many times are just rude responses. With 150,000+ members and growing, we may not notify a member prior to removing them from the group. This is something we rarely do, however name calling and continuing to be argumentative for the sake of stirring the pot will result in removal from the group. Also, do not post links to your personal YouTube channel. or Vlogs. They will be deleted. We do please ask that all members refrain from posting about illegal activity/policy breaking aboard CCL, or any cruise line for that matter. Our purpose here is not to teach anyone how to skirt regulations or smuggle booze. We firmly believe that smuggling booze hurts everyone in the long run, as reduced liquor sales will eventually cause higher cruise prices for everyone. Also, out of respect to the hard-working crews, we ask that no posts be made promoting tip removal. It is a hot topic, that never ends well. The crew work hard, and we fully support them. When commenting on someone's post please give accurate information. If you are not sure of something please look it up online or do not comment on the post. This helps eliminate wrong or illegal answers. Incorrect information will be deleted. Sometimes Carnival may deviate from their own rules which is an exception and does not mean that the same exception will happen for someone else. Personal experience doesn't trump specific information directly from Carnival, therefore Carnival will be the official source of information. No referrals for PVPs or TAs are to be made on the page, and doing so could result in removal from the group. If you are a travel agent or PVP, please do not solicit any members via pm.We want all members to feel comfortable posting and asking questions, without having many of the hundreds of TAs and PVPs here pming them. Also, no member may post a group cruise on behalf of a travel agent or PVP. We also ask that all members please refrain from posting items for sale, or links to solicit purchases from their home based business. We do our best to keep this page ad free. In the event of a man overboard or other tragedy on board a cruise ship, the administrative team will make one post, and no other posts will be allowed. Please don't block any Group Administrator or Moderators (see member list for names of the administration team) You may dislike us but you can be banned for this.

                 TPG Family
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to TPG Family! If you’re always looking for ways to make travel more fun, less stressful and less expensive for you and your family, this group is the place to be! What is TPG Family about? If you follow Mommy Points, you'll already have an idea. Think, using points and miles to make travel more affordably, but optimized for families. Whether that's the best credit card perks for families, the best hotel redemptions for family trips or special points bonuses for children, this group is meant to help make family travel easier, and make possible trips that you never thought you'd be taking. Within this group we invite you to post your personal tips and award stories, share your findings of points or travel-related deals, ask for advice on complicated travel itineraries, and more. Summer will be contributing regularly to TPG and to this group, TPG Family. Together we will help you and your family travel farther, longer and for less! Related topics include all things at the intersection of family travel, points and miles and having young kiddos! All posts should be relevant and respectful to all members of the group. If you are new to credit cards we invite you to visit our site (www.thepointsguy.com) for all the information needed to get you started. Any posts containing explicit language, graphic violence, sexually explicit material, or calls for boycott of a business will be promptly removed. Any sort of bullying or intolerance of one’s lifestyle is strictly forbidden. This includes, but is not limited to: religion, race, gender, sexual identity and age. All posts within the Lounge must have no intent to advertise or profit from a service or business. (This includes personal credit card referral links) Any sort of sale within TPG Family is strictly forbidden. All points, memberships, upgrades, or passes offered within the community must be done free of monetary exchange. Trading of benefits is subject to the rules outlined by the individual programs within which you are a member. TPG does not support any illegal trades, or arrangements that violate the terms outlined in each program. If TPG suspects you are engaging in any violation of our Lounge guidelines, we will terminate your access to TPG Family immediately.

                 Welcome to “EVERYTHING Disney Theme Parks”. If you are a collector, fan, enthusiast, imagineer, illusioneer, animator, cast member, zealot or newbie, you are welcomed here. Please feel free to share your fondest Disney Theme Park obsession (e.g. memories, stories, collectibles, photos, videos, selfies and wishes). Every one of them will all be revered, admired and cherished here. In this group we cater to ANYTHING and EVERYTHING that has to do with any Disney Theme Park Resort, Celebrity Sports Center, Disney Cruises, The Aulani Oahu Resort, Adventures By Disney and The Walt Disney Family Museum but only these venues from past, present and future. Please remember that we're all in this together to create a welcoming and "Family Friendly Oriented Group". Let's treat everyone with respect. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. Make sure everyone feels safe. BULLYING of any kind isn't allowed, and degrading comments about things like race, religion, culture, sexual orientation, gender or identity will not be tolerated. And please refrain from the use of the following: displaying naked photos, offensive material, foul language, political opinions, reporting unsubstantiated rumors from any Disney Cult Blog sites or shocking news regarding illnesses, deaths or “CRAZY” things witnessed at a Disney Theme Park and/or any other non-Disney Theme Park. In the event of such abuse your posts will be removed. If this conduct should continue, you will be banned from this group. Please do not block the admins, EVER! Even though you know who they are from the group's Description. They see "ALL" even if you think by blocking their view. ANY member new or existing from this group that blocks one of our Administrators will be BANNED IMMEDIATELY! This group is not to be used as a platform for selling things, advertising things for sale, basically ANY kind of advertisement which include discounted hotel room accommodations, special discounted admissions for any theme park (Disney or otherwise). Any such posts will be removed. Promoting someone's personal blog / vlog, YouTube Channel Subscription or website is simply not allowed. If these are posted they will be removed. This Group's Admin Team members are: - Gregg Ziak (Creator &amp; Founder) - Michael Kouri - Richard Kuchar - Stephen Ysmeal - Gern Blandsten Jr. (aka Dan Bejma) - Mike Marshall - Jim Batten This group is not associated or affiliated with The Walt Disney Company or it’s subsidiaries.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ANSWER THE QUESTIONS UPON REQUESTING TO JOIN.... Please answer the questions in order to be admitted. This is a Group for people who passionately loves Maui. Place to share photos and interact with each other. * New Members: Please answer the questions posed in order to join the group. The request to join will be declined if questions are not answered. * New members: Aloha &amp; welcome! Please introduce yourselves to the group and let us know where you are from. All members: * Please always be helpful &amp; polite to those asking questions in the group; please refrain from over-posting daily. Respect &amp; Aloha: * We want everyone to enjoy this group as we all have a mutual LOVE for MAUI. Respect is very important in the Hawaiian culture. Please practice ALOHA when posting &amp; commenting. A = Akahai meaning kindness (grace). To be expressed with tenderness. L = Lokahi meaning unity (unbroken) to be expressed with harmony. O = Olu’olu meaning agreeable (gently) to be expressed with pleasantness. H = Ha’aha’a meaning humility (empty), to be expressed with modesty. A = Ahonui meaning patience (waiting for the moment) to be expressed with perseverance. Promotion/Ads: * Can only be posted in the comment section in direct response to a question asked by a member or if a discussion has been started by the Admin where businesses are invited to post their links. Otherwise, the post will be deleted. Condo rentals: * Can only be posted in the comment section in direct response to a question about rentals. Otherwise, the post will be deleted. Fundraising Links: * These posts will be deleted as this is not really the group for that. Admin may decide on exceptions depending on circumstances. Mahalo to Kerri Wadsworth Grobowsky for putting our guidelines in writing.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 *** PLEASE READ BEFORE JOINING *** This is a group for WOMEN ONLY ~ This is a fun, supportive group of diverse, wonderful women who love to travel alone whether by plane, train, RV, boat, bicycle, backpacking, motorcycle or car … or dreaming about traveling solo. We are a chatty group which is encouraged. There are a bazillion TRAVEL and RV groups that stick to just that topic. This isn't one of them. If you wish ONLY travel posts, this group is not for you. I want this group for everything we women want to talk about… from leaving behind old lifestyles and embracing new ones, to travel wardrobes, music, travel plans, gadgets, tips and tricks, families, our fears, and our triumphs! We discuss our lifestyles and how we can get out of ruts and run with the wind. Do NOT join to PROMOTE your business or yourself ~ You will be removed from the group if you post or comment with promotions. I have once again stopped admitting travel agents. Always a few who spoil it for everyone. Do not ask members for contributions in any form ~ surveys, tips, guest writers, etc. I initiate a thread the last day of each month for members to post their personal blogs, vlogs or pages. That is the ONLY acceptable time. NO LINKS. Read the posting rules to learn how to post an article you want to share. And NO GIFS in a thread ~ makes a thread 12 miles long and very distracting to follow. WE ARE NOT A GROUP FOR YOU TO FIND SOMEONE TO TRAVEL WITH. We don't give tour or group advice. This is solo travel only. Exceptions are in the posting rules. Do not ask for information or post to the group with regard to traveling with others. ~ exceptions are in the rules such as an aged parent or small kiddos ~ Members do meet along the way. Just say where you are or where you are going. Great pals have have been made from member meet ups all over this beautiful world. Do not request Ex-Pat advice. There are Facebook groups who specialize with such information. SWT is for solo traveling advice. I CAN NOT APPROVE BLANK OR SPARSE PROFILES. If you have your profile with very strict privacy settings, you must PM me to tell me a bit about yourself. I want to keep our great group ~ great. If your name is written in non-English, please change it to this format: English first and then your name in the other language. That way I can tag you as I am limited to an English keyboard Due to our size and the love of spammers ~ all posts are set to admin approval. I sleep HAH! from midnight until 8am USA Central Standard Time. Please don't post Thanks for the Add type posts .. a post to introduce yourself with where you are is wonderful! however. &lt;3 Carolyn

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Disneyland Club 33
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Club 33 is a private club located in the heart of the New Orleans Square section of Disneyland. Officially maintained as a "secret" feature of the theme park, the entrance of the club is located next to the Blue Bayou Restaurant at "33 Royal Street" with the entrance recognizable by an ornate address plate with the number 33 engraved on it. When riding Pirates of the Caribbean, just as the ride departs, the Blue Bayou restaurant is visible, but the balconies above it are actually a part of Club 33.
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Disney Vacation Club Neighborhood
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Disney Vacation Club Neighborhood, the official Disney Vacation Club Facebook Group. Disney Vacation Club is Disney’s version of vacation ownership. Disney Vacation Club Members and guests gather here to freely ask and answer questions about the magic of Membership, sharing tips and insights based on their personal experiences, with no interjection from Disney Vacation Club itself, except as set forth in the Page Rules below. Whether the stories shared in this group help you get more from your Membership or simply learn more about Disney Vacation Club, welcome home. PAGE RULES: This group is a place for Disney Vacation Club fans to connect with each other. Disney Vacation Club will be monitoring the content of this group to ensure it adheres to our guidelines, however, we will not be actively engaging in member posts/discussions. To engage with Disney Vacation Club Cast Members, we invite you to visit the Disney Vacation Club Facebook Page. By participating in this group, you are agreeing to abide by the following rules: We reserve the right to remove any material that we find off-topic, inappropriate or objectionable. Links from third-parties will be allowed in the group, provided they are appropriate and on-topic. We do not accept or consider unsolicited idea submissions and, also, we must reserve the right to remove any posting that we deem to be an unsolicited idea submission. No solicitation, selling or advertising of any kind. No profane language, spam, offensive content or harassment. Content that is deemed inappropriate or is in violation of our standards may be removed by our moderators. Repeat offenses may result in removal from the Group. In joining this group, you acknowledge that any content uploaded by anyone other than Disney Vacation Club is the creation/views/responsibility of the submitter, and not Disney Vacation Club. This group was created to provide an inclusive environment for people to ask questions and share thoughts about Disney Vacation Club. Given some recent posts and comments that do not reflect the values of this group, we are requiring all posts be approved by the group admin before they are published. We will do our best to approve posts in a timely manner. Please review the page rules to understand what topics will be approved. Thank you for understanding.
