                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 DISNEYLAND ADDICTION
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Disneyland Addiction! IF OUR FOCUS DOESN'T FIT YOUR INTERESTS, THEN THIS IS NOT THE GROUP FOR YOU. Many of us have a very strong connection to Walt’s original park, and this is the place to pay homage to it. You are welcomed as ohana (family) here, so feel free to express your love and obsession for the park. Share anything related to Disneyland here: family photos/videos taken at the park, memories and observations of vintage, current, and future Disneyland, new or missed attractions, merchandise, food, etc. &gt; GROUP RULES &lt; Each member is responsible to READ AND UNDERSTAND the Disneyland Addiction (DA) policies. Breaking our simple House Rules may quickly land you permanently outside our gates. * Group Focus * We enjoy many facets of Disney, but topics outside this group’s scope are not permitted. Disallowed topics include, but are not limited to: - DCA or other Disney parks - Downtown Disney - Other hotels - Random and/or generic Disney clip art, memes, or videos - Non-Disneyland Disney news - Posting links to apps, groups, or websites other than official Disneyland content * Citizenship and Conduct * - Be kind to your fellow addicts, always. - Posts and membership requests are moderated. If your post or comment has disappeared, it violated a policy, or something in the thread triggered the thread's removal. - Share a handful of photos by grouping them in your OP. Use the Create Album feature to share many pictures at once. - Controversial topics will likely not be approved; if approved, and the conversation becomes heated, the thread will disappear. - The "Dirty Laundry" clause: manage concerns with fellow members and admins via PM. We keep things neat 'n pretty onstage, and ALL MEMBERS are "onstage" here. &gt; INSTANT BAN: - CALLING OUT FELLOW MEMBERS OR ADMINS OR BASHING THE FOCUS OF THIS GROUP - Blocking any admin - Sales, solicitations, promotions, or cross-promotion of other groups (including Disney fan groups). Note: DA merchandise and admin-approved posts may, at times, be offered) JOINING DISNEYLAND ADDICTION AND CONTINUING TO REMAIN A MEMBER SERVES AS NOTICE THAT YOU HAVE READ, UNDERSTOOD, AND AGREED TO THESE POLICIES. DA admins reserve the right to revise these rules from time to time. This group is NOT affiliated with The Walt Disney Company or Disneyland Park. Group founder- Gil Gomez ADMINS: Kathy Bullock Eva Williams Frank Michael Lawrence Gus Luttrell Gil Taimana Rick Kess Nicolette Amette Lynn Swearse Danny Miller Instagram: @disneyland_addiction Thanks for joining us! LET THE ADDICTION CONTINUE!!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the TPG Lounge! We're here to make your life easier. We trust you’ve been visiting the TPG site and soaking in all the tips, tricks and information explaining the essentials of points, miles and credit card usage. As a member of the Lounge, in addition to exciting members-only opportunities, you now have access to virtually mingle with tens of thousands of other travel savvy individuals who share your same enthusiasm for points &amp; miles. Within this group we invite you to post your personal reviews and award stories, share your findings of points or travel related deals, use one of our several travel recommendation threads to ask for advice. We may use your responses in editorial posts. Together we will help maximize award travel and get you to your next destination sooner than you think! We want to keep questions more advanced than beginner-level, as most beginner questions can be answered on the TPG site, elsewhere online or with a quick phone call. As the community grows, we continue to improve our curation and helpfulness: like group "franchises" that provide dedicated platforms to all group members to participate in conversations that matter to you, including (but not limited to) asking specific questions that would otherwise not be approved to the group if posted on their own. Lounge Rules &amp; Guidelines: This group is to allow real time communications of points and travel related information between TPG enthusiasts. Related topics include: hotels, airlines, lounges, mistake fares, points &amp; miles usage, member meetups, and travel deals. All posts must be relevant, and respectful to all users of the forum. If you are new to credit cards we invite you to visit our site (www.thepointsguy.com) for all the information needed to get you started. We reserve the right to share stories, photos and content posted here to our website and other social channels. Any posts containing explicit language, graphic violence, sexually explicit material, or calls for boycott of a business will be promptly removed. Any sort of bullying or intolerance of one’s lifestyle is strictly forbidden. This includes, but is not limited to: religion, race, gender, sexual identity and age. All posts within the Lounge must have no intent to advertise or profit from a service or business. (This includes personal credit card referral links) Any sort of sale within the Lounge is strictly forbidden. All points, memberships, upgrades, or passes offered within the community must be done free of monetary exchange. Trading of benefits is subject to the rules outlined by the individual programs within which you are a member. TPG does not support any illegal trades, or arrangements that violate the terms outlined in each program. If TPG suspects you are engaging in any violation of our Lounge guidelines, we will terminate your access to the TPG Lounge immediately.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Disney Annual Pass Holders &amp; Fans!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! This group is designed for ALL Disney (World Wide) fans and annual pass holders to get together, plan Disney outings, share Disney news, post pictures and chat about our past, present and future Disney adventures! The only requirement here is that you love Disney and are in touch with your inner child just like Walt Disney himself was! Whether your passion for Disney comes from The Disneyland Resort in California, Walt Disney World in Florida, Disneyland in Paris, Hong Kong Disneyland, Tokyo Disney, Disney Cruise Lines or even the upcoming Shanghai Disneyland, this is the place where everyone can be a child once again! NOTE: Please for everyone's enjoyment in this group there is absolutely no advertisements or selling of any merchandise permitted. If you post an advertisement in this group it will be immediately deleted, you will be removed and permanently banned/blocked from rejoining the group in the future and reported to Facebook for deletion. Thank you in advanced and enjoy!! About the Founder: Marty Ross has been an annual pass holder ever since he was a child. He is a former cast member, D23 Member, Disney Vacation Club Member with properties in Florida and Hawaii, owns shares in Disney stock and has been a very active participant in Run Disney events. In January 2014, Marty ran the Walt Disney World Dopey Challenge. This challenge consisted of a 5K, 10K, half marathon and full marathon on four consecutive days totaling 48.6 magical miles! He has also ran half marathons on the West Coast and has achieved is coast-to-coast challenge medal. Marty has traveled on all four of the Disney Cruise Line vessels; the Disney Magic, Disney Wonder, Disney Dream, and the Disney Fantasy. Marty also sings and his been invited into Club 33 to perform for celebrities and Disney Legens during the Christmas season. Marty has seen the park change throughout the years and was there on that very day when they placed the time capsule into the vault in front of sleeping beauty's castle back in 1995. Marty plans on being there at same day in the year 2035 when they open up the time capsule. Marty has a huge love for Disney artwork and his favorite character has always been Pluto. Marty can replicate the voices of Mickey Mouse and his good friend Goofy. Marty is a great source of Disney information and history so please don't hesitate to reach out and ask him if you have a question. Marty's favorite Walt Disney quote is: "Laughter is timeless, imagination has no age and dreams are forever." ~ Walt Disney ~

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Crown &amp; Anchor Facebook Group. Please like the official Crown &amp; Anchor Page: fb.com/RoyalCaribbeanCAS The purpose of this group is to provide a positive forum for those who love cruising with Royal Caribbean. We are here to exchange information and experiences of enjoyment. We want to keep this a positive forum and request that everyone be kind to others who post, with no harsh or harassing words. Members may have views/opinions that may differ from yours, so don't get into back and forth rants trying to convince someone that yours is the best view. You're welcome to post negative posts, as long as it's constructive and may benefit others. This page is monitored and posts which generate ill will, as well as spam and other derogatory posts, will be deleted immediately and the poster removed and banned from the group. TOPICS: Everyone feel free to ask a question or start a topic, whatever is on your mind concerning cruising with Royal Caribbean and/or the Crown &amp; Anchor Society. (We really don't want to hear about those other cruise lines so don't mention them). No posting/promoting other Facebook groups or outside travel sites/blogs. PHOTOS: Please don't use our group wall as your personal photo album. (i.e. you and your significant other drinking a cocktail - or feet out to the H20, etc.) Personal pics will be removed from the wall. You can post photos in response to questions, but please don't use the wall to post personal photos to start off. Please don't post pictures of it snowing outside, clothing, jewelry, temp screenshots, countdowns to your next cruise, memes, etc. We are all excited for your next cruise, but these types of photos are just repetitive and unnecessary. You're welcome to post photos of ships (in/out), ports, or general locations that everyone can enjoy. If you want to add batch photos, create a photo album using the "Photos" tab. If you are a sales or travel agent, this is not the site to solicit or mention your business; any inappropriate posts will be deleted. Travel agent referral by members is also not allowed. This is also not the place to try and sell items, jewelry, clothing, etc. *The admins of this group may remove comments and/or posts, close threads, a remove or ban members at their discretion and without notice. This is an unofficial group, not managed by Royal Caribbean. THANK YOU AND HAPPY CRUISING!

                 We Are Travel Girls
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to WE ARE TRAVEL GIRLS!! We Are Travel Girls is a global travel community created to inspire, connect, educate and empower female travellers around the world. Founded by Becky van Dijk and Vanessa Rivers in 2016, We Are Travel Girls connects women online at WeAreTravelGirls.com and shares daily travel inspiration on our popular Instagram @WeAreTravelGirls. An integral part of our community is also bringing women together offline by hosting We Are Travel Girls Meet Ups and Travel Girls Getaways around the world. Who is a travel girl? Travel girls are women of all ages. They are women of every colour and ethnicity, from every walk of life, mothers and daughters, sisters and friends. They are women from all over the world wanting to connect through travel - women looking for inspiration to have the courage to chase their dreams. It's women just like you. JOIN THE WE ARE TRAVEL GIRLS COMMUNITY! ~ GROUP RULES: We don’t want to have a tonne of rules in this group, but we ask politely that you use this group for the following: DO: - Post your travel tips, informative travel articles, travel questions in the group, occasional requests for help to win a trip - Connect with other women in the community and plan to meet somewhere around the world! DO NOT: - Create follow me threads for any social media channels. These will be removed. - Promote your own company or brand on this page. If you wish to promote your destination, brand, product please contact us at contact@wearetravelgirls.com to discuss this. If you post here, your post will be removed. - Arrange un-official WATG meet-ups in your area under WATG name without express permission from the owners. Please contact us if you are interested in events contact@wearetravelgirls.com ABOVE ALL treat each other with respect, any members who are rude or aggressive will be removed. For any questions please contact Becky van Dijk or Vanessa Rivers directly or email us at contact!@wearetravelgirls.com ~ Contribute Your Travel Story: WeAreTravelGirls.com/Contribute Subscribe To The Blog: WeAreTravelGirls.com/Subscribe Events Announcements: WeAreTravelGirls.com/Events Join Our Travel Girls Getaways: Getaways.WeAreTravelGirls.com Find Us At: Web: WeAreTravelGirls.com IG: Instagram.com/wearetravelgirls P: Pinterest.com/wertravelgirls T: Twitter.com/wertravelgirls

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! This Facebook Group is created for CouchSurfers in the greater Los Angeles area! Visit our sister groups too: West Los Angeles: http://www.facebook.com/groups/couchsurfingwla/ Long Beach: http://www.facebook.com/groups/couchsurfinglb/ Orange County: http://www.facebook.com/groups/CouchSurfingOC/ San Fernando Valley: https://www.facebook.com/groups/LosAngeles.SFV/ If you got stranded or can't find a couch within 3 days of your arrival, try the emergency group: https://www.couchsurfing.com/groups/11809 We're a very active, fun group so anyone, CouchSurfer or not, is welcome to join if you're interested in meeting locals and visitors to LA and finding fun things to do here! We look forward to seeing you at one of our events! **Make sure to arrange couch requests thru the actual CS site where you can view each other's profiles and references. Not everyone in the Facebook groups are actual couchsurfers. This group is created as an all-inclusive, safe space for all members. We are dedicated to providing a harassment-free experience for everyone, regardless of gender, gender identity and expression, sexual orientation, disability, physical appearance, body size, race, age or religion. We do not tolerate harassment of participants in any form. This includes, but is not limited to: - Violent threats or language directed against another person. - Discriminatory jokes and language. - Posting sexually explicit or violent material. - Personal insults, especially those using racist or sexist terms. - Unwelcome sexual attention. - Repeated harassment of others. In general, if someone asks you to stop, then stop. Because the nature of the CS community, hosting and interaction is based on trusting strangers and honorable conduct, mutual safety and respect is the biggest priority. Members asked to stop any harassing behavior are expected to comply immediately. If a member engages in harassing behavior, the admins may take any action deemed appropriate, including expulsion from the group. If you have been harassed in this group or in relation to it, please contact one of the admins or myself directly: https://www.couchsurfing.com/users/1666889/profile Please do not post other member's CS profiles here without their knowledge. We do not condone public shaming of people and their personal online profiles without their knowledge or ability to defend against attacks. If you are being harassed or have negative interactions with a CSer that is documented on the site, either on forums, references or private message, you can contact the Safety team here: https://support.couchsurfing.org/hc/en-us/requests/new?category=safety (Harassment policy updated 08/01/15 by T.Nguyen, group creator.)

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Disney Parks for Plus Sized Guests
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Vacations for Plus-Sized (18+) people can be nerve-wracking. This group is for Disney lovers to ask questions &amp; share advice &amp; experiences about their vacations as it pertains to being a person of size so that we can all have a WONDERFUL experience! This includes things like walking to prepare your body for miles of walking in the parks, comfort or size of beds, how a restraint works on a ride, plane seats, etc. There are a few RULES and they are the same on each board: 1) Keep it NICE. We already deal with a myriad of self-image issues. This should be a safe place! We have no tolerance for shaming, bashing, ridiculing, etc. Honesty is appreciated, but you can be honest in a helpful way or a hurtful way. Words can tear people apart. If you wouldn't want it said to you, don't say it to someone else. 2) No posts concerning weight loss or dieting. We want this to be a safe place without fear of judgement. Not everyone who is larger is uncomfortable with their weight! Don't mention weight loss in your posts - having lost weight or trying to lose weight. Posts can always be written without this information. Posts that mention weight loss will be deleted without warning. 3) No spamming/advertising of other pages or groups including YouTube, blogs, Etsy shops or anything that can you can generate you money. This includes as comments to posts and in unsolicited private messaging. Also, NO GIFT EXCHANGES CARD EXCHANGES OR GIVEAWAYS ON THIS BOARD WHATSOEVER WITHOUT PERMISSION. 4) The creator of this page, Sheila Nowell, is a full time travel agent. We know that not everyone in this group will use her services, but PLEASE don't advertise or promote another travel agency in your posts or comments or private messages as a courtesy to Sheila unless you are specifically asked. Sheila has to make a living, too! :) (With that being said, don't hesitate to ask Sheila about her FREE planning services at any time) 5) MEETUPS - the admins and moderators of this page do not promote meetups. However, if you wish to form a meetup with other board members, please do so at your own discretion. We take no liability of the actions or peril of those who meet up. If you believe one of the rules above is being broken, hit the "Report Post" option. That will automatically inform an admin or moderator to determine if it should be removed or not. While you can copy and paste one of the above rules as a comment on a post that may violate rules, please don't try to be an admin. :) Many people telling someone their post is not allowed can really be a downer! Follow the rules and this board will remain an awesome place. Thanks, everyone! Have fun!

                 We are Marriott Bonvoy Platinum, Titanium and Ambassador and those of Lifetime elite members group. ----- We were originally SPG (Starwood Preferred Guest) Platinum Group since 23 September 2016 and were later combined with Marriott/Ritz-Carlton Platinum. Then now we are Marriott Bonvoy Platinum, Titanium and Ambassador and those of Lifetime elite members group. Platinum, Titanium and Ambassador Elite members and those of Lifetime elite members are welcome to join. Further, Marriott Bonvoy officials are also welcome. - ----- We have some rules to keep in mind: - This is NOT run by Marriott Bonvoy officials but by non benefit Marriott Bonvoy fan administrators . - Please write in English always but don't hesitate to write imperfect English by non-English speakers. - Please allow imperfect English written by non-English speakers. - Share any info or news you hear about SPG, let's keep everybody informed. - Support all users in a helpful manner. Everyone has an opinion. It may not be yours but please respond in a POSITIVE and SUPPORTIVE manner. -When you post, please write easier words and avoid unnecessary/unfamiliar abbreviate words or too professional terms as well as common slang in order to make our discussion to be shared with every member especially for new comers, non-English speakers and unprofessional members. - Be advised some people may be new to everything so we are here to help them not crucify them. - Please note DO NOT advertise other Marriott Bonvoy groups here if exist, although any other Marriott Bonvoy group member, website or business persons are welcome to join and post on this group. - We encourage users to express themselves. However, comments that harass, intimidate, threaten or are otherwise deemed as not supportive will result in an immediate banning of the user. This is not a place to denigrate Marriott Bonvoy users or Marriott Bonvoy as a company. There other venues for that if you are so inclined. -Basically you can post with URL linkage of your own or others Instagram, Facebook or album blog pages related with Marriott Bonvoy but please don't include personal business engagement such as affiliate or buy/sell offers in them. - No foul language or insults. - No Affiliate Links - No selling/buying - Have fun and keep the conversation going!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Vegan Travel
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Making travelling as a vegan easy. Travelling is awesome, new countries, new languages, new people and new experiences. But as a vegan it can sometimes be a bit scary. Let's help each other out, ask questions and get answers. POSTING GUIDELINES – 1. All posts must be related to vegan travel. No recipes, fundraisers, general vegan activism debates, etc. There are tons of other vegan groups for that. 2. Be respectful. Not everyone will agree on everything but you can have a discussion in a polite way. This means no name-calling, shaming, bullying, harassment, etc. No blocking or disrespecting of admin and moderators. Disrespecting another member will lead to automatic removal. 3. Absolutely zero tolerance for disrespecting any culture, religion, race, gender identity, sexual orientation, etc. Disrespecting another member will lead to automatic removal. 4. No excessive posting of promotional content to the main feed. You may post vegan travel content ONLY, and keep your blog/youtube, etc. shares to once a week MAX. Excessive and off-topic promo will be deleted, you will be given a warning, and if you don't abide then you may be removed. 5. Use the search bar before posting to see if your question has been answered. This is a large group and some destinations are asked about very frequently (Berlin, London, NYC, etc). We have resource pages for popular cities - please see announcement for direct links. 6. No direct messaging members without their permission. Harassing members will lead to removal. If you repeatedly violate these rules you may be removed without warning. Please read this detailed list of guidelines for further clarification on the above short rules: https://docs.google.com/document/d/1XUVP8Rj9HK8ZxPmURdoufTDImCLYkItAu9zCOO0H9a4/edit?usp=sharing
                </div>

                 Princess Cruises - Passenger Forum
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Princess Cruises - Passenger Forum! For new members: please note, this is NOT an offical Princess Cruises page. If you are looking for employment with Princess Cruises, you will need to contact them through the official Princess website - https://www.princess.com/ This group is however, for any one who has cruised, or is planning to cruise. with Princess Cruises. People cruising all sectors of the world are welcome to join our Forum and discuss their cruise travels, the cruise lines and other cruise related topics. Feel free to share photos of your travels, ship and shore experiences, and to ask advice from peers and enjoy discussing and planning your next cruise holiday in a relaxing and supportive atmosphere. While this group encourages people to have an opinion, and values opinions from all members, please remember to express yourself in a courteous and respectful manner. Anyone making personal insults, indulging in name calling, engaging in combative commentary or posting inappropriate content will be removed. Additionally, while all people in travel related occupations are welcome (including PCL crew members), this group has collectively decided that there will be no advertising, direct soliciting, hawking or sales pitches allowed in this Forum without prior approval of the Admin team. Please refrain from posting any advertising content, including advertising of your personal businesses, commercialised blogs and/or other Facebook Groups. Thanks and happy cruising!

                 Welcome to Families Who Love to Travel! This page is a safe space for parents worldwide to ask questions, provide guidance, and exchange travel ideas, itinerary suggestions, concerns, or experiences. Families Who Love To Travel often compiles information posted here to aggregate and publish on Families Love Travel, our community-based website (www.familieslovetravel.com) focused on kid-friendly travel around the world. Families Love Travel is written by parents, for parents - detailing advice on hotels, restaurants, and family-friendly activities throughout a variety of popular destinations. Whether it be contributing to our Facebook group or writing for our website, Families Who Love To Travel invites anyone willing to recount their story to become a member of our growing community! Before posting, just remember to please be respectful to other members! Also, feel free to add anyone else you think would be interested in the group. With your support, we can grow this family-friendly travel community into a global network! We’re all here to help each other. Thanks for contributing! Honestly, we couldn’t do this without you.

                 *** PLEASE READ THE RULES!**** Carnival Cruise Chat’s “Rules of Getting Along” Carnival Cruise Chat is intended to be a friendly Facebook page to help those that have cruising questions as well as for those experienced cruisers that enjoy talking about all things cruising. Toward that end, a few basic rules for everyone to follow- This used to be a much shorter list... 1) Be nice. Attacking other posters will not be tolerated. Yes, we can all enjoy spirited discussion of opinion but out right attacking of other members will result in someone being “unfriended” 2) Keep it clean please. We can’t control the age of those on this page so in interests of being family friendly please refrain from bad language. 3) No soliciting, spamming or advertisements. Do Not PM our members or ask members to PM you so you can sell them anything! Including your travel agent services or those of your good friend.... 4) Please no posting of Travel Agents or Carnival PVP names. TAs or PVPs posting of their services will be removed from the group. 5) DO NOT POST links to other Facebook groups or links to outside cruising sites please. Only FB links allowed are for Roll Call pages and cruise radio dot net. 6) No links to YOU TUBE videos. We don't have time to review them for spam. 7) Please no posts about how to break the rules on Carnival. Not because we are rules police but because we have found that many people can not be civil when it comes to discussions on such. &lt;- Can't BELIEVE I had to add that rule 8) No politics or religion! I don't need to read about your viewpoints any more than you want to read about mine. Everyone will get a long better without discussing it.

Our goal is to see how far our Ducks will travel and where their journey might take them. Keep or hide, you decide, but please post your Ducks travels here so everyone can enjoy. When posting, “Hide” include a pic and which ship you started it’s journey on, same goes for when you “Find or Keep”. You can use any type of “Rubber Duck”, just add the Facebook logo and page name to bottom so others know where to go So get your ducks in a row and let’s see how far they go! No Promotion of or Ads for any type of service allowed! Never take your ducks and toss overboard. No Negative post or comments. And don’t forget,... you must answer the questions.

                 A spin-off from the orig Disney Planning Mamas group - This is a private group for anyone who wants to chat about DisneyLAND USA vacations for families... reviews, planning advice, etc. We only talk Disney on here- so I will delete any other types of posts just to keep the board on topic. Reporting a post gives a message to check it out and we will decide to delete or not, etc. Since we can't be on 24/7, this helps me keep the board clean, and more enjoyable for everyone! :) -Do not post about being a Travel Agent at all - feel free to answer posts as anyone else would - but if you mention being a TA, having clients, or ask anyone to PM you, or if you PM them- you will be removed from the group. -Do not post anything for sale here. If you do- you will be removed from the group. We have a spin off selling group you can join to sell Disney related items. https://www.facebook.com/groups/Disneyresellgroup/ -Do not post links to your personal websites or blogs. We are not here to help you get hits..... you will be removed from the group. -No unsolicited PM's, you will be removed from the group. -You may post links to articles that help answer questions someone asks... but again, do not link to personal blogs/sites. -Stay on topic- anything that is not Disney related will be deleted - there are lots of other great boards for general discussions... this one is -this board is family oriented, so if you don't have kids, you will likely get bored of our child talk here. -If someone asks for a TA recommendation, people may rec one they have used - but TAs may not promote themselves. -We have a few other spin-off groups from this board you are free to join... to help keep DLPM more on topic - more detailed discussion of the following can happen on these boards.... ******Disney Crafting Mamas, for ideas/help with making your own Disney crafts https://www.facebook.com/groups/1470283153195761/ ******Disney Running Mamas, for those DPMs who are runners, planning Disney marathons, 10K, 5K, etc. https://www.facebook.com/groups/573705849314647/ *******Disney Cruising Mamas, to discuss cruise specific details https://www.facebook.com/groups/707130349349441/ *******Disney Military Planning Mamas, for all our awesome military families to discuss plans with specific military discounts, Shades of Green, etc. https://www.facebook.com/groups/232843183568005/ 
                </div>

The price you pay is not affected. In addition to various retailer affiliate programs, we are also a participant in the Amazon Services LLC Associates Program, an affiliate advertising program designed to provide a means for us to earn fees by linking to Amazon.com and affiliated sites.                  DVC - Disney Vacation Club
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Facebook's largest independent DVC group! A fun place for DVC Members, future members and Disney Fans, in general, to discuss their love for DVC and Disney. We ask that you be kind and respectful of one another. Enjoy! Group Rules: 1) No Travel Agent or DVC rental service advertising or solicitation of any type without permission from the Administrator. When posting, please do not name your Travel Agency or DVC Rental Service outside of the DVC Rental Store. Posts will be deleted by admins. Please respect this rule or you will be banned. Please DO NOT contact members privately based on something they posted in order to solicit. Soliciting/PM members for this purpose will get you banned. This includes telling a member to PM you. 2) No advertising or solicitation of any type by individuals without permission from the Administrator. This includes soliciting the rental of DVC points or reservations. Posts will be deleted by admins. Please DO NOT contact members privately based on something they posted in order to solicit. Soliciting/PM members for this purpose will get you banned. This includes telling a member to PM you. 3) We will remove any topics or posts we deem inappropriate or disruptive to our group. These include rudeness, profanity, personal verbal attacks on other members or just general ongoing "Snarkiness". This group will not be that kind of group. 4) No solicitations for donations. 5) No advertising your personal groups or pages or sharing links for them UNLESS approved by admin. 6) If you need assistance with another group member, please ask an admin if you are having a particular problem or being harassed. Please remember everyone here has a passion for Disney and we can share it positively. 7) Giveaways may be posted ONLY with the admins permission. 8) If you link or share a post to a blog or website which has another travel agency sponsor or DVC rental service other than the DVC Rental Store then it will be removed. 9) Any threads deemed to be unacceptable by the admins will be deleted without notice. 10) Do not block any of the Administrators of the group. This hinders our ability to view posts and to police the group to keep it safe for everyone. 11) You will want to contact one of the Administrators before posting if your post begins with, "Please remove if not allowed" or "Please let me know if not allowed". In most cases, these posts are against the rules and the opening statement is a subtle way of sneaking it in. Almost without exception, these type posts will be removed.

We kindly ask that you refrain from naming Travel Agents, Travel Planners, Big Box/Wholesale Stores that sell travel and/or Travel Agencies. Do not self-identify as a Travel Agent. This includes on the group page and via private message. Also, on the same subject, our membership is currently NOT open to Travel Agents. There are plenty of other groups that sell Disney Travel. We prefer a sales-free zone in our group and try to protect the privacy of our members. DISNEY OFFICIAL LINKS. No links to any Disney site that is not ‘Official’ Disney, this includes unofficial blogs, guides, other Facebook pages, etc. Some links that are allowed include: This group’s web page Official Disney sites Official government sites (used to clarify travel rules and regulations) Links listed at this groups web page SALES/SELLING. While we do allow members to share information on where they purchase Disney treasures, We DO NOT allow members to sell/buy merchandise in the group, refer to the fact that they sell, or post links with referral codes. Also, no promoting your spouse, friends or neighbors. We DO NOT allow ANY web links to Zulily, Amazon, Shave Clubs, credit card offers, or any independent reseller on-line sites. Why? The aforementioned online shopping websites allow resellers and we do not allow self-promotion within this group. Screenshots, WITHOUT links, of items from such online shops are permitted. This entire guideline applies to both the Facebook page and via private message. ONLINE BEHAVIOR. Any person who belittles, bullies or otherwise makes another member feel uncomfortable, either at the Facebook page or via private message, may be removed from this group, as well. We understandably take a Zero Tolerance stance for such behavior. BLOCKING. You may not block any Admin of this group. If you do so, and do not remove the block upon request, you will be removed from the group. NOT DISNEY-RELATED? Any threads that have nothing to do with Disney will be deleted. SCREENSHOTS. Posting screenshots of private message conversations between ANY members. Thank you Mark

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Tips for Special Needs at Disney
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! This is a group that I designed for sharing tips for Walt Disney World, Disneyland, the Disney Cruise line, Universal Studios, Sea World, Legoland, and other amazing destinations. This page is for sharing tips, strategies, and ideas that have helped my family and my guests in the past. My goal is to build a place safe for families to ask questions and learn on how to help their family have a magical vacation. I am a Disney planner that specializes in helping families with special needs plan their dream vacations. I also book Universal Studios, Cruises and Sandals Resorts. Please contact me if I can help you plan your next vacation: Robyn Adams Take My Hand Travel 404-277-0212 TakeMyHandTravel.com NEW MEMBER REQUESTS!! IMPORTANT PLEASE READ! Please be aware that we are currently experience a very high volume of new member requests (well over 125 per day). Michelle is the admin responsible for approving new requests and she is trying to handle them all as quickly as possible. Be aware that we do have a policy of checking the profile of each new member and we require that all 3 questions are answered. If any of the 3 questions are unanswered or your profile is locked for privacy then we will deny membership. You are free to re-request membership at any point. If you are unable to access all the questions, please try on another device or send Michelle a message. The current wait time to gain membership is approximately 3 weeks. If your trip is more than 1 month away we ask that you be patient and we will approve your membership as quickly as possible. If your trip is within 30 days please send a message to Michelle and she will approve your request as quickly as possible. Upon gaining membership to this group, please make our pinned post your first stop! Our main goal is to protect the privacy of every member in this group and to make sure that all members are here for the same purpose: to share tips and support for those with Special Needs traveling to Disney. If your goal is to find potential clients or sell a product or service this is NOT the appropriate group for you. Note to travel agents requesting membership: The owner of this group is Robyn Adams of Take My Hand Travel. Robyn has spent many years and endless hours helping members of this group whether they are clients of hers or not. This group is not meant to be a place for you to solicit clients or learn the ins and outs of special needs travel. There are other Facebook groups and websites for that. Previously this group was open to travel agents but we have been forced to end that policy due to the deceptive practices of a few. If you have any questions, please contact Michelle or Robyn directly. *This policy applies to travel agents only. If you work in the travel industry in another capacity, please just let us know by answering the third question but you will be allowed in the group.

                 This group is an extension of the GothicRosie's Disneyland Information Page and is mostly for the Disneyland Resort and Anaheim Resort Area (DLR/ARA) but posts about other parks may be allowed if they relate to the DLR/ARA. Group Rules Any posts, comments, and/or members are subject to removal from the group for a violation of the rules listed below. Do not post “Delete if not allowed” because it probably isn’t and will be deleted. If you want to be sure something is ok, re-read these rules or PM an admin. Respect other members and admins and treat each other as you would have them treat you. MUST ANSWER QUESTIONS WHEN REQUESTING TO JOIN GROUP. 1. Be Kind, Courteous, and Keep It Disney and Family Friendly 2. No Hate Speech (against race, religion, sexual preference, basically anything), Bullying, or Trolling 3. No Religious or Political Posts 4. Do Not Moderate Comments or Posts on Your Own. Use the “Report Post to Group Admins” found by clicking on the little dots (...) on the top right of a post for anything offensive or breaking a rule. 5. No Promotions, Affiliate Links, Spam, Personal Social Media Promotions, Go Fund Me or other Charitable Request Posts, and no Giveaways Unless Admin Approved 6. Respect Everyone’s Privacy and Do Not Send Unsolicited PMs to Members 7. Do Not Block Admins 8. No Buy/Sell/Pick up Offers/Pickup Requests/Trade Requests or Private Services Offers such as Travel or Personal Shopping. The group has two authorized Personal Shoppers if you need their services please contact them directly at Piglet’s Treasures ( www.facebook.com/pigletstreasures/ ) or Disneyland_Goonies ( www.facebook.com/Disneyland_Goonies-1950922538536958/ ). The group also has a Disney Authorized Travel Agent, Brandy McQueen, and if you need her services please contact her directly on her Facebook Page: www.facebook.com/TravelPlannerBrandy/ Admins are not responsible for any transactions between a member and these vendors. 9. No Offensive Material, Profanity, Sexual Innuendo/Content, or Drug Related Content. Please Keep it Disney! 10. Don’t Ask/Beg for CM’s to get you into the parks or into Company D 11. Don’t Ask/Beg for Members to get you into Club 33 in DL or Club 1901 in DCA This group is not affiliated with Disney, Facebook, Instagram or their affiliates. Admins reserve the right to revise these rules from time to time.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Mixtries (Girls LOVE Travel ®)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ** To Join ** • Must be a member of Girls LOVE Travel • Click Join Group • Answer the 3 questions that appear when you request to join ---------- Mixtries is for all Women of Color (WOC) as well as all their allies to have a safe haven within the larger Girls LOVE Travel community. This subgroup is NOT an exclusionary group. ANY member of Girls LOVE Travel is welcome to join subject to the standard GLT subgroup approval process. (click to join then email Mixtries@gmail.com to be approved) Mixtries provides an avenue to have an open community in which concerns, feelings and hard truths can be discussed in a tolerant and loving manner. The other GLT subgroups exist to address topics that touch the hearts of a good portion of our members but aren't necessarily for all GLT members. Within those subgroups, members have been able to form tighter bonds utilizing a more intimate setting. This enables those members to get the support and friendship they need in that area while still maintaining the ability to be active members in the main GLT group. The same principle will apply here. WOC have topics that touch their hearts and souls that Non-WOC are unable to fully understand the magnitude of simply bc we have not walked in their shoes. It has been said multiple times - "This group is for travel. WHY do we "have" to allow these topics to be addressed etc etc?" ... Why? ... Because yes first and foremost Girls LOVE Travel has transcended being merely a travel group. Girls LOVE Travel is a COMMUNITY. It is a sisterhood that travels with LOVE and kindness. WOC members are GLT members whose voices have expressed not being heard. It is important to stress that WOC does not mean Black Women Only. It means Black women, Latina women, Indian women, Asian women, etc etc - as well as their allies. Any member of our group that has felt silenced, you have been heard. Mixtries is home base for the issues that WOC have been calling to be addressed... welcome. 
                </div>

                 She Goes Places is focused on empowering female travelers world-wide. Through shared stories and experiences, it is our hope to celebrate the lives of women around the world. If there are comments or posts that are considered offensive or seen as a way to bully other group members, they will be removed. Our hopes are to promote an inclusive environment free from the constraint on the basis of culture, race, disability, sexual orientation, expression, age, religion, family structure or relationships, or economic status.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Aloha Guy’s, this page’s mission is to provide a peaceful and constructive place to enjoy what we all love and that’s our ownership in MVCI. Also, it's a link while we are away from “home” reading posts and enjoying pictures. Together over the years we have discovered much and shared our knowledge willingly especially when someone needed helpful suggestions as well as getting the best use out of owning MVCI. We do not allow rentals or sales because the FB format is too restrictive and not of interest to the general group. This page’s mission is not to become a complaint page beyond some reasonable and informative information that may help a fellow owner avoid a problem or direct them to the proper place to get help. We never allow attacking each other and only allow respectful conversation that enhances what we share MVCI. Politics is not allowed! we all have perfectly thought out points of view, so, no reason to enlighten anyone with comments or replies and we will remove those posts and the poster 😊. We have 10 Monitors that love MVCI and we watch over this page as best we can and assist the best we can. But we also remove some at times when they become overly disgruntled, just plainly looking to troll, agitate or looking for trouble. We’ve found it’s best not to confront and we just remove them from our group and sometimes with a ban. Please if you see a problem post report it and we will do our best to keep this page an enjoyable place to enjoy our “home” when we are not “home” Mahalo

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Disney Park Fan Base
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Disney Park Fan Base. This group has been designed as a place for fans to gather and share their Disney Theme Park experiences, stories, memories, feedback, hints, tips and even frustrations, with each other. We have created a fun and welcoming environment, where people are free to be themselves. We are a "grown-up friendly" group of fans who are passionately enthusiastic about Disney theme parks. "Grown-up friendly" means we welcome spirited discussion and even debate as long as it is respectful. Unlike other groups, we don't barrage our members with rules and reminders about how to behave. The guidelines for this group can be found by clicking the rules section. Like the vast majority of Disney fan pages, this group is not affiliated with the Walt Disney Company in any way. We believe in maintaining an intimate and exclusive environment. It is not the intention of this group the be the largest Disney fan group. Just the best. This page will grow with an emphasis on quality content and members over the quantity of either. About the Founder: This group was created by Jerry Vargas. A lifelong fan of Walt Disney and the theme parks that carry his name, Jerry is a student of Disney history. He is a former Disneyland Resort Cast member, and has been a Disney Store Manager, and a Disney Vacation Planner. On July 17, 2015, Jerry accomplished something very few people have achieved, when he visited every Disney theme park in the United States in a single day. This Disney "bucket list" achievement was done on the day of Disneyland's 60th Anniversary. We’re happy you’ve chosen to join this group, and we encourage you to invite your favorite Disney friends to be a part of our world. © 2020 JVP Travels

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Truly Vintage Disneyland II
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for fans of Walt Disney's Dream, his first Theme Park, known around the world as the best, most intimate and most Magical Kingdom of them all Disneyland. But we are OK with members going "Off Topic" here and there, as long as it doesn't dominate the theme of a thread. I started this group after feeling frustrated with other Snooty, Controlling groups who don't allow their members to network or discuss their concerns, wants or changes to the Disney resorts. Bah Humbug was their attitude, I wanted to be in a group where we can speak openly, without disrespect to members opinions...But have candid conversations. To Me, Face Book is a Social Media site, and there's no reason we shouldn't network together within the vein of the theme. So, in this group we allow networking, posting vintage or current photos of Disneyland, Walt Disney World, and other aspects of the Disney empire, but our main focus is on Disneyland Anaheim itself. We're also open to our members sharing their newest books, read, or written, tours they've taken or are giving, other Disney groups they belong to, or created, BUT I ASK All Members To ask My permission Before Posting Invitations to other Groups. Our members aren't interested in SPAM and postings listed without permission will be Deleted or Reported to me or my admins as Spam. If you have been granted permission to post in our group, I ask not to Over Post your groups- Members complain about "over posting." Thanks! : ) Advertising not pre-approved will be deleted and members can be banned for life! Yikes! You’ll find photos and stories from the early years &amp; perhaps some more recent experiences, at Disneyland many of our members work or have worked at Disneyland or the Disney company who love this park as much as we do, please be respectful to them. This group is dedicated to knowledge, past and current history. Unlike other groups: We allow our members to talk about New items the park sells, and/or older items sold at Disneyland. You'll see pieces of Vintage Disneyana collections, Its fun to share these treasures of Disneyland's past, educating those in the future. I welcome you to post your own vintage photos, or those found online, but encourage you to give photo credit when posting other people's pics. We also allow current photos of you, your family &amp; friends at Disneyland today(which will be Vintage Tomorrow). I will not tolerate being accused of breaking my own rules here. If you aren't happy with the content posted, Please contact me through a P M w/your concerns. I'm open minded and fair. Badgering or accusing any of the admins in the open forum will cause permanent removal. Be open minded when reading other people's comments, don't assume they're negative. Since we are Texting/not Talking we cannot "hear" the sentiment in comments(many of which are meant to be silly, and funny). Thanks for joining us, now let's have some good old fashioned Disney fun!

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Coco Palms Resort, Kauai
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Coco Palms Resort on Kauai opened in 1953 with 24 rooms, when Grace Buscher was hand-picked by Lyle Guslander to become the resort's first manager. It was the location of the famous outrigger canoe wedding scene from Elvis Presley's Blue Hawaii, released in 1961, the resort was also used in many other films, such as South Pacific, Pagan Love Song, and the TV series "Fantasy Island”. It was the world's most famous Polynesian resort until hurricane Iniki struck Kauai on September 11, 1992. The Coco Palms was severely damaged by Iniki and the resort was left to decay for almost two decades now. The costly repairs and insurance issues left the Coco Palms officially closed with no announced plans to reopen. The current owners had a plan to rebuild the resort with condos, but the current economic climate has made it difficult. The resort is up for sale now, anybody what to partner up and invest? Weddings are still available on the famous lagoons where the “Blue Hawaii” wedding scene took place under the coconut palms. Limited tours are conducted by Hawaii Movie Tours. Groups still make pilgrimages to Coco Palms to have their photos taken in front of the little grass shack where Elvis once stayed, or in front of the huge conch shell a the entrance. The Coco Palms property is the ancestral home of Kauai's Alii (royalty) since the 13th century, the area encompassing the Coco Palms Resort was the home of Kauai's last reigning queen, Queen Deborah Kapule, in the mid-1800's. The famous 2,000-tree coconut grove was originally planted with coconut tree nuts imported from Samoa by Mr. William Lindeman in 1896. Hurricane Iniki data: http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hurricane_Iniki Hawaii Movie Tours: http://www.hawaiimovietour.com/ Photos and videos posted on this site by members become the property of the administrators of this site and my be reused in whatever manner they see fit to help benefit the site or for any other reason. *we are not supported, endorsed nor affiliated in any way with the Coco Palms Hotel, its developers or investors, or any organization or individuals. But we'd like to be. ;-)
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Scottish Travel Society. Our group was founded with a love of Scotland, coupled with the desire to aid others in planning a trip to, and visiting, this beautiful country. Our members come from all over the globe and share a commitment to showcase the very best (and sometimes, the worst) of what this ancient land has to offer. We welcome your stories and pictures of your travels, and our members all pitch in to provide a huge pool of information along with ideas, suggestions, and tips for making your visit to Scotland, a dream come true. Our "files" section has an extensive list of links to everything you may need to help in the planning of that perfect vacation. From Accommodations to the Zoology of Scotland, we have tried to provide solutions to any questions you may have about traveling to Scotland and whatever your needs may be concerning the details of your trip. Please feel free to explore the links and ask any question to which an answer may be a bit harder to find. We have also included a list of "must see" places, arranged geographically to help give you some ideas about what to do or where to begin. Please read the Pinned Post for a short list of rules concerning posting to the group and some suggestions on how to make your search more productive and enjoyable.

(=3 This group was originally created on Meetup.com on April 22th, 2008, and is about real people for real people. We all share a passion for Disney related things. The Founder/Administrator (J.C. Tregarthen) and co-administrative members of our group (Ron DeViso, Marc Nakao and Alex Inigo) accept people, not bots. Well, at least, we try. Most of the times we get it right... Many of us feel comfortable in coming to "The Happiest Place On Earth" - either alone or (preferably) with others - to enjoy the days, nights and other things that are happening throughout the resort and the local hot spots - The HOB (House Of Blues), The Mad Hatter Tea Party, The Jazz Kitchen, wine tasting at DCA, late nights together at Trader Sams after the parks close, etc. Here's YOUR chance - and our opportunity to share and join in our upcoming events, birthdays, fine dining, concerts at the Mad 'T (DCA), Tomorrowland Terrace and HOB... whatever may strike your fancy in all-things Disney. Again ~ we welcome you to our Disneyland Pulse (DLP) Family, and looking forward to meeting you and creating some longtime friendships and lifetime memories at the parks together... and beyond!
